{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","title":"POWER RANGERS TIME FORCE Is a Well Crafted Soap Opera","link":"https://geektyrant.com/news/power-rangers-time-force-is-a-well-crafted-soap-opera","description":"<figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597976537940-JM24K6CGYNTFSBR0P8W1/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kJg-Fs9N0laGvgucVyy6WKsUqsxRUqqbr1mOJYKfIPR7LoDQ9mXPOjoJoqy81S2I8N_N4V1vUb5AoIIIbLZhVYy7Mythp_T-mtop-vrsUOmeInPi9iDjx9w8K4ZfjXt2drbhfxOw7I34SIWe0zvJ4VjHWRgBYKlgdVaKn5VvPEh8ZDqXZYzu2fuaodM4POSZ4w/image-asset.jpeg\" data-image-dimensions=\"1920x960\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f3f2fd98e07611554f087ed\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597976537940-JM24K6CGYNTFSBR0P8W1/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kJg-Fs9N0laGvgucVyy6WKsUqsxRUqqbr1mOJYKfIPR7LoDQ9mXPOjoJoqy81S2I8N_N4V1vUb5AoIIIbLZhVYy7Mythp_T-mtop-vrsUOmeInPi9iDjx9w8K4ZfjXt2drbhfxOw7I34SIWe0zvJ4VjHWRgBYKlgdVaKn5VvPEh8ZDqXZYzu2fuaodM4POSZ4w/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">Well, I just finished watching <strong><em>Power Rangers Time Force</em></strong>, adapted from <strong><em>Mirai Sentai Timeranger</em></strong>, recently. The season is one of the more popular ones and for good reason. I would say that it takes the dramatic approach from <strong><em>Lightspeed Rescue</em></strong> and kicks them up a notch. I mean, come on, you’ve got Jen trying to figure out which version of <strong>Jason Faunt</strong> she loves. If that’s not a soap opera, I’m not sure what is. So, shall we really dive in?</p><p class=\"\">The core episodes of <em>Time Force</em> are really good for the most part. I do feel that there are some problems with it though since they do bring in that meddlesome device called time travel. The main story is that Jen, Lucas, Katie, and Trip are members of Time Force in the year 3000 and go against orders to chase the evil mutant Ransik back to the year 2001. Ransik’s goal is to destroy humanity in the past before Time Force is a thing that can stop him. Once in the past, the four members of Time Force find Wes, who looks exactly like Jen’s fiance whom Ransik just murdered in the year 3000. Turns out his DNA matches and he’s able to become the Red Ranger and allow the others to become the Pink, Blue, Yellow, and Green Rangers respectively. They defeat Ransik’s mutants and eventually capture him.</p><p class=\"\">Let’s talk about Ransik first. His real motivation is basically, humans in the year 3000 don’t like mutants and treat them poorly so the humans are scum. Granted, I guess he’s not entirely wrong. I just wish that we were shown actual cases of this instead of just seeing him as a mutant hobo in flashbacks. We’re repeatedly told that he was mistreated and therefore humans must pay the price. It’s okay motivation, I just wish there had been a bit more of his case built up. It just feels too generic to me. However, Ransik is played by <strong>Vernon Wells</strong> (<strong><em>Mad Max 2</em></strong>) who does give a good performance.</p><p class=\"\">Continuing with villains, I hate Nadira, Ransik’s daughter. She is just annoying and extremely shallow. She has no growth until the 3-part finale and because it happens so late, I’m really left even more annoyed. All she cares about for 90% of the season is shopping/stealing stuff like clothes and jewelry. Then, in the finale she helps a woman give birth (how does she know how to help?) and suddenly she’s questioning everything she’s ever thought about humans. While this can be the case, it felt rushed at the very end. I know I give<em> Lost Galaxy</em> crap and don’t like it very much, but Trakeena showed a lot of real growth over time and was easily one of the best parts of the season. Seeing such a downgrade is disappointing to me.</p><p class=\"\">Frax is the final villain to really talk about. This is an interesting one. I found his personal story interesting with his hatred for Ransik after Ransik almost murdered Frax as a Human which led him to become a robot. He then joined Ransik with the plan of betraying him later down the road. What I don’t get is why we never really got the Frax vs Ransik bout that was building up. Frax eventually leaves Ransik’s side to do his own thing, but is then found before then and brought down to be reprogrammed. This creates some interesting moments for him when he sees Nadira trying to change and not hate. However, Frax’s whole thing is that he is wanting to bring down Ransik, yet is constantly helping him. I feel like it would’ve made more sense at this point to have Frax not use the X-Vault mutants that would be very helpful to Ransik, but rather keep seeing Ransik fail with the weaker mutants. Then, defeat Ransik when he’s weak after fighting the Rangers.</p><p class=\"\">OK, so what’s going on with everything else? Well, the filler episodes range from really stupid and dull to fun but not great. I will admit that I actually do enjoy “Nadira’s Dream Date” although that’s mostly for the way that Ransik acts. Also, “Movie Madness” was a lot of fun to watch. “Beware the Knight” is an example of a terrible filler though. Also, the crossover episode was a bit of a mess in my opinion.</p><p class=\"\">The big problem with the main story, meanwhile, is the use of time travel. First, I don’t think they do enough time travel in general. There should’ve been more of that. However, you also keep having the weird paradoxes of them traveling back in time to save the future, but they use the <em>Back to the Future</em> logic where changing the past changes the future. However, they then have no changes that we’re aware of actually happening in the future? The future is set in stone, but they can still alter it? It doesn’t make a lot of sense. That being said, the overall writing, directing, and even acting are really good, especially for a Power Rangers season.</p><p class=\"\">Another thing I don’t really like is that Alex somehow survived Ransik’s attack, to then become like the head of the Time Force operations with the Rangers. However, it seems at first that he’s having to act in the shadows and secretively with people not knowing that he is still alive and doing things, but then the Time Force captain acts like Alex is the one in charge. That was a bit of a disconnect. This is also all ignoring the fact that Alex is a tool.</p><p class=\"\">Eric is another character I don’t like. He’s just a jerk, and they wait until the finale to actually explain what his motivation is. Throughout the season we see him putting on this stubborn and tough act while still (almost) always doing the right thing in the end. We could have and should have learned his motivation way earlier in my opinion without cramming it in with everything else happening in the finale.</p><p class=\"\">OK, let’s stop being negative and go positive. I’ve already talked about how I enjoyed the core storyline, some filler episodes, and a lot of the acting. Well, I do also appreciate that the Megazord has two different modes. I like it when Megazords are versatile like that. I also love that their secret base is in a clock tower. That’s very on the nose and I love it. Another thing I really appreciated was that the Rangers were secret, but there were people who knew, like Eric and Wes’s dad (played by <strong>Edward Laurence Albert</strong> who gives possibly the best performance of the entire season). This gives the Rangers a little more freedom in some areas as far as what can be said/done but still restricted to help create drama. It’s also a way to help Mr. Collins undergo some serious character development throughout the season.</p><p class=\"\">The finale, “The End of Time,” is pretty good as well. I don’t think it’s as good as some other finales due to the fact that it decides to cram in Eric’s motivation, Nadira’s whole character arc, and some big battles. However, I did really like the way that Wes and Eric team up and they become the last standing forces for humanity for a while. It really adds to the drama and makes sense. They’re the only Rangers from the year 2001 and they’re not going down without a fight. Of course, the other Time Force Rangers come back from the future to help them, but then they really struggle against Ransik, who only surrenders after hurting Nadira who’s trying to protect a human baby. It’s pretty cheesy.</p><p class=\"\">Oh, also, the clip show wasn’t super dumb for once! That’s right, there’s a clip show episode, but when they’re not showing clips (which they keep to a minimum), they’re advancing the plot! It’s a miracle! I actually enjoyed “A Calm Before the Storm” because it was setting up “The End of Time” beautifully while doing a freaking clip show! Why couldn’t previous seasons be this smart?</p><p class=\"\">If I had to pinpoint a theme for <em>Time Force</em>, it would once again be about destiny. However, instead of <strong><em>Lost Galaxy</em></strong>’s theme of fulfilling one’s destiny, <em>Time Force</em> is about creating your own destiny. Wes is constantly told that he can’t change destiny, but at every turn he and the other Rangers end up doing just that. They even inspire Alex to bend the rules and change history a little (see my earlier complaint about time travel not working well).</p><p class=\"\">All in all, I did enjoy watching <em>Time Force</em>. It was fun to revisit after almost 20 years. Sure it has its flaws, but it does have quite a lot of positive things going on for it. While it’s not my favorite, I do understand why so many fans have it so close to their hearts.</p><p class=\"\">Current Power Rangers Ranking:</p><ol data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Power Rangers In Space</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Power Rangers Zeo</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Power Rangers Time Force</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Power Rangers Beast Morphers Season 1</p></li><li><p />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">For those of you bummed out about all the Halloween events being canceled this year, you’ll be happy to learn that there’s a<strong><em> Stranger Things</em></strong> drive-through experience coming to Los Angeles in October!</p><p class=\"\">The <strong>Stranger Things: The ‘Drive-Into’ Experience</strong> is an interactive theater show co-produced by Netflix and Fever. </p><p class=\"\">Attendees will be safely quarantined in their vehicles, “which they will use to literally drive through various different sets, stopping for extended periods as actors and special effects bring scenes to life around them. As scenes come to an end, the convoy will be ushered into the next location, as a new convoy takes their place. Each convoy will consist of 24 cars.”</p><p class=\"\">The experience will last an hour long and will include recreations of the Starcourt Mall, the Upside Down and the Russian Labs. They will also be setting up visual and auditory aspects to reflect the 1980s setting, and some of the show’s characters will pop up during the show.</p><p class=\"\">Greg Lombardo, head of experiences at Netflix, said in a statement:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“Stranger Things has always been larger than life and we wanted to flip the world upside down for our fans. So buckle up like Billy is driving, keep your eyes on the neon lights, and steer clear of the shadows because there’s no telling who or what you might come across in Downtown Los Angeles this October. Whatever you do, don’t get out of your car!”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Secret Cinema is behind the creative direction of this new event. A waitlist is available now on the&#160;<a href=\"https://strangerthingsdriveinto.com/\" target=\"_blank\">event website</a>, and tickets will go on sale August 26th. So if you want in on the action, you better get on that list!</p><p class=\"\">Source: <a href=\"https://variety.com/2020/tv/news/drive-through-stranger-things-experience-los-angeles-1234741532/\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">Director <strong>John Carpenter</strong> is partnering up with Blumhouse&#160;Productions and producer <strong>Jason Blum</strong> to develop a reboot of Carpenter’s classic 1892 sci-fi horror classic <strong><em>The Thing</em></strong>. I hate this news. Even with Carpenter involved, this just leaves a bad taste in my mouth. </p><p class=\"\">Seriously, why in the hell couldn’t Carpenter and Blumhouse team up to develop an original project!? Why did it have to be a reboot of an all-time classic that should never be remade?! This makes me sad.</p><p class=\"\">Carpenter announced the news this past weekend on a panel for the Fantasia International Film Festival. During the Q&#38;A  Carpenter was asked if he had talked with Blum about directing any projects and he said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“I have? I don’t know about that. But we’ve talked about — I think he’s going to be working on ‘The Thing,’ rebooting ‘The Thing.’ I’m involved with that, maybe. Down the road.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The project is still in the early stages, and no other details have been revealed. Don’t forget, there was a prequel film that was released in 2011, which starred <strong>Mary Elizabeth Winstead </strong>and <strong>Joel Edgerton</strong>. I honestly don’t really remember anything from that movie. I had to watch the trailer to be reminded.</p><p class=\"\">It’d be fine if this new project turned out to be another prequel that told a different story or even a sequel, but I just can’t get behind a reboot of the original film, which was based on  1938 novella “Who Goes There?” by John W. Campbell Jr. I love that film.</p><p class=\"\">The story for<em> The Thing</em> centers around an Antarctic research team who find themselves fighting for their lives as they are being terrorized by a parasitic alien life form that can imitate other people.</p><p class=\"\">What are your thoughts on Carpenter looking to reboot <em>The Thing </em>with Blumhouse?</p><p class=\"\">Source: <a />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">It’s been made very clear that director <strong>Andy Muschietti</strong>’s <strong><em>The Flash </em></strong>is going to break open the DC multiverse in big and exciting ways. Bringing <strong>Ben Affleck </strong>and <strong>Michael Keaton</strong> back to reprise their roles as different versions of Batman is just the tip of the iceberg.</p><p class=\"\">In a report from&#160;<a href=\"https://www.vanityfair.com/hollywood/2020/08/ben-affleck-returns-batman-the-flash-multiverse-keaton\" target=\"_blank\">Vanity Fair</a> it’s explained that the plot of<em> The Flash</em> will see Barry Allen&#160;\"breaking the bonds of physics to crash into various parallel dimensions, where he’ll encounter slightly different versions of DC’s classic heroes.\"</p><p class=\"\">The director of the film went on to explain things a little further regarding how this new DC Multiverse is actually going to work, saying, “All that you've seen exists.” He says:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">\"This movie is a bit of a hinge in the sense that it presents a story that implies a unified universe where all the cinematic iterations that we’ve seen before are valid. It’s inclusive in the sense that it is saying all that you’ve seen exists, and everything that you will see exists, in the same unified multiverse.\"</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">So, the multiverse that was explored in the&#160;<em>Crisis on Infinite Earths</em>&#160;crossover is real and relevant, and everything from&#160;Superman&#160;to&#160;The Dark Knight to&#160;Green Lantern, and more have&#160;all happened and are canon in their own respective realities. I assume that also means <em>The Joker </em>and <em>The Batman</em>.</p><p class=\"\">This is sure to be a complicated concept for people who are not familiar with how this all works in the comic books. While <em>The Flash</em> is the focus of&#160;the<em> </em>movie, it sounds like anything goes, anything and any cameo is possible as&#160;Muschietti explores the DC universe with<strong> Ezra Miller</strong>'s Flash leading the story.</p><p class=\"\">What other things are you hoping to see in The Flash that you know anything can The first trailer for <strong><em>The Batman</em></strong> dropped during DC FanDome and it’s now online for you to watch and enjoy over and over and over again! This is the trailer that fans have been super excited about seeing, it’s what I was looking forward to most from this DC fan event and it does not disappoint! DC definitely saved the best for last! </p><p class=\"\"><em>The Batman</em> trailer delivers something incredible and totally unexpected! We finally get to see what exactly what Reeves and the stars of the film have been teasing all these past months in their interviews and it gave me the chills. This team of talent is going to deliver fans something special and totally awesome! I loved what I saw and I can’t wait to see more! </p><p class=\"\"><em>The Batman</em> will be a noir-style film that will lean into Batman in his detective mode. The director said that it’s going to tell a deep and psychological story and confirmed that the movie will not be an origin story. However, it will acknowledge his origin and how it’s still something that he’s “majorly struggling” with. As you’ll see, Batman is also relentlessly brutal when he fights! </p><p class=\"\">There will be a series of murders and crimes that start taking place in Gotham and as Batman investigates those things, they begin to reveal the darkness of Gotham City to him. It’s also <a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/the-batman-is-said-to-be-a-character-based-movie-focusing-on-alfred-and-batman\" target=\"_blank\">been said</a> that this is a character-driven story that will focus on the relationship between Bruce Wayne and Alfred Pennyworth. DC Films President <strong>Walter Hamada</strong> confirmed that this movie will tell the Batman “year two” story. </p><p class=\"\">When talking about the story Reeves said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“The idea is that we're in YouTube. It's the Gotham experiment, it's a criminal... experiment he's trying to figure out what he can do that can finally change this place. In our story, he's in that mode that's where you meet him and you see that he is charting what he's doing and it seems that he's not having any of the effect that he wants to have yet and that is when the murders start to happen and then the murders begin to describe sort of the history of Gotham in a way that only reinforces what he knows about constant. It opens up a whole new world of corruption that went much farther.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The film stars <strong>Robert Pattinson</strong> as Batman,<strong> Zoe Kravitz </strong>as Cat Woman,<strong> Andy Serkis</strong> as Alfred, <strong>Paul Dano </strong>as Edward Nashton/The Riddler, <strong>Jayme Lawson</strong> as Bella Reál, <strong>John Turturro</strong> as Carmine Falcone and <strong>Peter Sarsgaard</strong> as Gil Colson. <strong>Gil Perez-Abraham </strong>(<em>Orange is the New Black</em>), <strong>Charlie Carver </strong>(<em>Teen Wolf</em>), and <strong>Max Carver </strong>have also been cast in undisclosed roles. It’s so cool to finally see many of these characters in action! </p><p class=\"\"><em>The Batman&#160;</em>is now scheduled to hit theaters on October 1, 2021. Director <strong>Matt Reeves</strong> is going to give us one hell of a great Batman movie!</p><iframe scrolling=\"no\" data-image-dimensions=\"854x480\" allowfullscreen=\"\" src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/NLOp_6uPccQ?wmode=opaque&#38;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"854\" data-embed=\"true\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"480\">\n</iframe><p class=\"\">As for how the movie fits in with the rest of the DC multiverse, Hamada explaining that the existence of the multiverse allows Warner Bros. and its filmmakers to&#160;\"tell these great stories where we can tell different stories. There's one earth where have Gal and Ezra and another where we can have 'Year Two'&#160;Batman...and then there's Joker, which isn't part of either continuity.\"</p><p class=\"\">Hamada went on to tease future spinoffs and sequels saying, \"Matt Reeves can continue to build out his Gotham [in The Batman]. Those are things that we can do because we don’t have to worry about how that would impact <em>Aquaman 2</em> or <em>The Flash</em>, because it’s all just part of the Multiverse.\"</p><p One of the panels that I was super anxious for was for the movie, <strong><em>The Flash</em></strong>. The panel featured <strong>Ezra Miller</strong>, director <strong>Andy Muschietti</strong>, screenwriter <strong>Christina Hodson</strong>, and producer <strong>Barbara Muschietti</strong>. As I figured, there really wasn’t much info given other than this will take us into the Multiverse through the Flash’s amazing powers. Then we were given something that made my inner DCEU fan scream with complete unbridled joy. </p><p class=\"\">Near the end of the panel, director <strong>Andy Muschietti </strong>gave us some concept art of Ezra Miller’s new Flash suit, that you can check out above. I love how streamline and sleek the new design is. While I was still marveling over the new design, he casually announced that the new suit was made by Barry Allen’s new friend, Bruce Wayne. Then this image was shown:</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  \n\n    \n  \n    \n\n      \n\n      \n        <figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1598126969718-4JXYQHU55K7GHVB786M1/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kH4XpC1GoHhd9REVTWEcb99Zw-zPPgdn4jUwVcJE1ZvWQUxwkmyExglNqGp0IvTJZamWLI2zvYWH8K3-s_4yszcp2ryTI0HqTOaaUohrI8PI_2kcW2nJL0bOuShl24drZhmr1uJCkvaW1rprc0JnqbI/and+that+the+DC+Universe+will+be+born+out+of+Barry%E2%80%99s+story.+2\" data-image-dimensions=\"998x578\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"and that the DC Universe will be born out of Barry’s story. 2\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f417b4a2428047f12356d4e\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1598126969718-4JXYQHU55K7GHVB786M1/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kH4XpC1GoHhd9REVTWEcb99Zw-zPPgdn4jUwVcJE1ZvWQUxwkmyExglNqGp0IvTJZamWLI2zvYWH8K3-s_4yszcp2ryTI0HqTOaaUohrI8PI_2kcW2nJL0bOuShl24drZhmr1uJCkvaW1rprc0JnqbI/and+that+the+DC+Universe+will+be+born+out+of+Barry%E2%80%99s+story.+2?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">That is right folks, that is <strong>Michael Keaton</strong>’s Batman! We have heard previously that he is going to be appearing in the film, but we didn’t know what his role would be. Based on this picture, we can now assume he will be in at least one fight scene.</p><p class=\"\">The director also explained in the panel that the film will be a time travel story and explained:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“His mother was murdered, his father was trained and incarcerated, and all his journey from then was a man trying to make things right…the script really capture his loquacity, his personality…he’s someone who has the power of changing events of the past, but by doing so, can deteriorate the very fabric of the space-time continuum.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Hodson went on to say, “The cinematic multiverse is going to be born out of this movie. It’s born out of Barry’s story.”</p><p class=\"\">I cannot wait to see this movie. I have always been on the side of the fence that wants DCEU movies to succeed and now that I can see all of the pieces coming together, I couldn’t be more excited. Sequel","link":"https://geektyrant.com/news/russell-crowe-reveals-maximus-jesus-like-return-in-the-gladiator-sequel","description":"<figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image-dimensions=\"1920x1080\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f3e9d87b6e57c0a3a1f7616\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597939081629-KJFF88UVL3U5VXK5F3EN/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">When news got out that there was a sequel to<strong> Ridley Scott</strong>’s <strong><em>Gladiator</em></strong> being developed, a lot of people wondered why? and how? The first film was great and there was no need for a sequel, on top of that, <strong>Russell Crowe</strong>’s character died at the end, and the early concept for the sequel would have seen him return.</p><p class=\"\">At one point,<strong>&#160;Nick Cave</strong> was attached to write a&#160;<em>Gladiator 2</em>, <a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/ridley-scott-reveals-how-he-would-bring-maximus-back-for-gladiator-2\" target=\"_blank\">which would have</a> seen Maximus travel through the afterlife before being resurrected through a portal in the body of a dying warrior. The project is still in active development with producer <strong>Doug Wick</strong>, but the new story is going in a different direction that won’t involve Crowe’s resurrection. During a recent interview with <a href=\"https://screenrant.com/gladiator-2-maximus-return-death-story-russell-crowe/\" target=\"_self\">ScreenRant</a>, Crowe expanded on the original idea and how Maximus would have come back, saying:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">\"I haven't talked to Doug in a long, long time. Last time I talked to Doug, he said he had this great idea where Maximus gets carried from the stadium and they pull back this big rock and he gets put into this cave and then the rock closes over and he's anointed with oils. And then the rock opens up and he comes out. And I said, 'Doug, I don't think we have the rights to that story.' But that was a long, long time ago and I don't think he appreciated my sense of humor at the time.\"</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">As you can see, Maximus’ return sounds a lot like the resurrection of Jesus. Judging by Wick’s response to Crowe’s joke, Wick didn’t seem to like having the similarities pointed out to him.</p><p class=\"\">As for the sequel that’s currently in development, Ridley Scott would love to do it. According to Wick, “It's really all about getting something on paper. Everyone [involved with the original] loves the movie too much to ever consider cheaply exploiting it and making something that's a shadow of it. It's just really a clear creative problem, working on a script, and if we can ever get it to a place ... Ridley's working on it, it's really just a question of whether we can get it to a place where it feels worthy to make it. It's a real challenge.\"</p><p class=\"\">Producer <strong>Walter F. Parkes</strong> previously said that the story for the sequel would pick up “30 years later… 25 years later.” Three decades after the death of Maximus. It’s been said that it will follow the continuing story of Lucius, the son of Lucilla (<strong>Connie Nielsen</strong>)- “The youth was the nephew of Commodus (<strong>Joaquin Phoenix</strong>), the weaselly son of Roman leader Marcus Aurelius who murdered his father seized the throne and wound up in the gladiator ring with Maximus, who though mortally wounded, skewered the emperor before fading into the great beyond to reunite with his slain wife and son. Maximus saved the boy and his mother while avenging his own family, and left a strong impression on the young Lucius.”</p><p class=\"\">It’ll be interesting to see if this sequel actually ends up getting made. />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">Director <strong>Josh Boone </strong>(<em>The New Mutants</em>) has spent seven years working on developing an adaptation of Stephen King’s epic good vs. evil novel, <strong><em>The Stand</em></strong>. It started out as a four-part film project but it ended up evolving into a ten-episode miniseries which is coming to CBS All Access.</p><p class=\"\">During a recent interview with <a href=\"https://www.comingsoon.net/tv/news/1145928-exclusive-josh-boone-talks-his-the-stand-series-previous-attempts\" target=\"_blank\">Comingsoon</a>, Boone, who directed the first and final episodes, talked about his work on the upcoming series and also opened up about the previous attempts that were made to bring the story to life. Before Boone jumped on board, directors <strong>George A. Romero</strong>, <strong>Scott Cooper </strong>and<strong> Ben Affleck </strong>had tried to get it off the ground. When talking about the work they did on it, Boone said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“Getting to read Scott Cooper’s draft was awesome, it’s very different from the book but it’s very cool and it’s very Scott Cooper. There were some other drafts, like there was the Affleck drafts, I don’t think he was the writer of it but I know he was involved in the drafts. I read some stuff like that, I have always wanted to read the George A. Romero version, I’ve seen some storyboards of it, his Lincoln Tunnel storyboards. One of the best things we had is somebody who’s worked with Peter for years is our first AD, Nick&#160;Mastandrea, who worked on every George A. Romero movie, all the early Pittsburgh ones and through the ’80s. He was like horror royalty, so I had as many of those guys from when they made real movies with practical effects as I could.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">When talking about the tenth and final episode of the series, Boone said that King provided the series with a coda that wasn’t included in the novel and teased what fans can expect in the expansion of the story:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“King wrote us a lovely coda, which is sort of the story he’s wanted to tell for a long time that takes place immediately after&#160;The Stand<strong>&#160;</strong>that provides an additional resolution for Franny, who’s sort of not involved in the climax of the book, which I thought was really, really brilliant and a deeply moving script. I was so moved to get to go make it.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">I do love that the series will actually expand on the story of the book and go beyond where the story ends in the book. Here’s the synopsis for the series that was previously released:</p><p class=\"\">The ten-episode series adaptation reveals that this is&#160;the way the world ends: “with a nanosecond of computer error in a Defense Department laboratory and a million casual contacts that form the links in a chain letter of death. And here is the bleak new world of the day after, a world stripped of its institutions and emptied of 99 percent of its people. A world in which a handful of panicky survivors choose sides — or are chosen. A world in which good rides on the frail shoulders of the 108-year-old Mother Abigail — and the worst nightmares of evil are embodied in a man with a lethal smile and unspeakable powers: Randall Flagg, the dark man.”</p><p class=\"\"><em>The Stand</em> features a fantastic cast that includes<strong>&#160;James Marsden</strong> (<em>Westworld</em>) as Stu Redman, <strong>Amber Heard </strong>(<em>Aquaman</em>) as Nadine Cross, <strong>Alexander Skarsgård</strong> (<em>Big Little Lies</em>) as Randall Flagg, <strong>Greg Kinnear</strong> (<em>As Good as It Gets</em>) as Glen Bateman, <strong>Whoopi Goldberg</strong> (<em>Nobody’s Fool</em>) as Mother Abigail, <strong>Odessa Young </strong>(<em>Assassination Nation</em>) as Frannie Goldsmith,<strong> Nat Wolff </strong>(<em>Paper Towns</em>) as Lloyd Henreid, <strong>Henry Zaga</strong> (<em>The New Mutants</em>) as Nick Andros, <strong>Jovan Adepo</strong> (<em>Overlord</em>) as Larry Underwood, <strong>Owen Teague</strong> (<em>IT</em>) as Harold Lauder, <strong>Brad William Henke </strong>(<em>Orange Is the New Black</em>) as Tom Cullen, <strong>Daniel Sunjata</strong> (<em>Rescue Me</em>) as Cobb, a new character, <strong>Katherine McNamara</strong> (<em>Arrow</em>) as Julie Lawry, <strong>Eion Bailey</strong> (<em>Band of Brothers</em>) as Teddy Weizak, <strong>Hamish Linklater</strong> (<em>Legion</em>) as Dr. Ellis and&#160;<strong>Heather Graham</strong> (<em>The Hangover</em>) as Rita Blakemoor.</p><p class=\"\">Boone&#160;wrote the series along with<strong> Ben Cavell </strong>(<em>SEAL Team</em>) and King wrote the tenth and final episode of the series. released in theaters and became a classic to fans who saw and loved it. The film is a sword-and-sorcery fantasy that follows a warrior who can telepathically communicate with animals and goes on a journey of revenge alongside his animal allies. The movie is still beloved to its fans, and the people who made it, including director and co-writer <strong>Don Coscarelli</strong>. But he has a problem- the film is lost. The original negative is, at least, and he’s hoping you can help him.</p><p class=\"\">Coscarelli launched the website this week <a href=\"https://www.whereisthebeastmaster.com/\">www.whereisthebeastmaster.com</a>, and explained the situation to <a href=\"https://ew.com/movies/the-beastmaster-don-coscarelli/\">EW</a>:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“The rights holder sent [someone] to pick up the negative and the guy put it in his vault in the San Fernando valley. Then he sold the house and now he [doesn’t] know where it is. As they used to say in the labs, when we were making&#160;<em>Phantasm</em>, nothing’s ever lost, it’s just misplaced. We have this fervent hope that maybe we can reinvigorate this fan base of ours to go out and help find it.\"</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">So if you or someone you know has moved into a home in the San Fernando Valley, maybe look around for the missing original. It would mean a lot to Don Coscarelli, and it would make for a pretty good story! </p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  \n\n    \n  \n    \n\n      \n\n      \n        <figure class=\"\n 06:03:02","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","title":"BrainLeap Launches New Gaming Platform for Attention and Focus Challenged Children","link":"https://geektyrant.com/news/brainleap-launches-new-gaming-platform-for-attention-and-focus-challenged-children","description":"<figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597885022491-G9CCQW6UL02DVANVQVLC/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg\" data-image-dimensions=\"1920x1080\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f3dca5a1fcc7e2f1e1f86d8\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597885022491-G9CCQW6UL02DVANVQVLC/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\"><a href=\"https://brainleaptech.com/the-science/\" target=\"_blank\">BrainLeap Technologies</a> launched a new gaming platform all about helping children with attention and focus challenges. The platform called The Attention Arcade is a series of games specifically designed to help improve focus and attention skills. The games were created based on National Institutes of Health-funded research on the matter.</p><p class=\"\">In the pilot study from UC San Diego, 23 individuals between the ages of 9-25 were tested and played the games at home. At the end of the trial improvements were seen in fast and accurate shifts of attention, inhibitory control, and an improvement in focus. Each candidate noted an improvement in at least one area while “most showed improvements on multiple measures.” Another study by an independent researcher at University of Florida – Gainesville worked with 19 participants in an afterschool program. Once again, results were positive.</p><p class=\"\">Here’s what BrainLeap says about the research and The Attention Arcade:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">Research has shown that eye movement and attention are tightly linked and share much of the same brain circuitry. To put it simply, where we look and where we are planning to look are where we are placing our attention. The games in The Attention Arcade leverage this connection with games designed to train different aspects of attention. The player uses his or her eyes to control the games via an eye tracker.  Improvements are closely tied to the amount of time played. If a child is playing daily for 20 minutes or more, users can see results in as little as four weeks, with significant improvements possible after eight weeks.</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">There are six games included in The Attention Arcade along with a parent training module, a reporting tool to track what your children are playing and for how long, and three assessments to help “demonstrate the skills users are developing in the games transfer to skills in the real world.” You can purchase them all from <a href=\"https://brainleaptech.com/home-users/\" target=\"_blank\">BrainLeap</a> for $39 per month or you can get bunlde with the required eye-tracker for $49 per month and a $100 refundable deposit. The eye-tracker is also available separately on <a href=\"https://www.amazon.com/Tobii-Eye-Tracker-5/dp/B0897GCBWW/ref=psdc_172511_t1_B01MAWPMXQ\" target=\"_blank\">Amazon</a>.</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">DR. MOLE &#38; MR. HIDE - The goal of Dr. Mole &#38; Mr. Hide is to hit bandit moles as they pop out of the ground and to avoid looking at the professor moles. As the game progresses, the moles appear more quickly and from more locations. The game trains the ability to quickly and accurately orient the player’s gaze and attention to a sudden event, and to monitor a wide range of view. As the game gets harder, inhibitory control is also developed as the player avoids looking at the professor moles.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">SHROOMDIGGER - The player searches for spotted-top mushrooms in a mystical landscape. Focusing gaze on a “shroom” causes it to shrink until it disappears with a poof. Find all the shrooms before time runs out!  The game trains attention by requiring steady fixation of gaze, visual search in a crowded field, and the ability to ignore moving distractions.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">SPACE RACE - The player uses gaze to steer a ship through a cosmic race course, aiming for green gates, avoiding red gates, and collecting stars for bonus points. The game trains anticipatory focus by requiring the player to gaze ahead of the current ship position. Executive functions related to planning are trained by the need to quickly decide whether collecting a star will leave enough time to avoid a red gate that causes damage to the ship.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">KUNG FALL - The player trains a ninja for the Dojo’s Aerial Skills exam. Using gaze, the player guides the ninja to land and balance on a series of rock pillars while avoiding birds and ignoring falling cherry blossoms. The game trains planning, steady fixation of attention and gaze, and the ability to ignore moving distractions. This game is unlocked after 3 hours of play.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">BUTTERFLY BOB - Butterfly Bob flies through a peaceful landscape, collecting nectar from flowers while avoiding menacing bugs and traps hiding in bushes. The player uses gaze to guide Bob vertically, flying higher or lower as needed. It trains anticipatory focus, planning, and prioritization. This game is unlocked after 6 hours of play.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">TRAPPED-A-ZOID - The player uses gaze to steer a spaceship to avoid colliding with neighboring ships. It trains inhibitory control of attention, requiring the player to suppress salient visual input while gazing into the empty space where the spaceship will be safe. Executive function is trained by engaging top-down strategy planning. This game is unlocked after 10 hours of play. </p></li></ul><iframe scrolling=\"no\" data-image-dimensions=\"640x480\" allowfullscreen=\"\" src=\"//www.youtube.com/embed/172RBqsjLzU?wmode=opaque&#38;enablejsapi=1\" width=\"640\" data-embed=\"true\" frameborder=\"0\" height=\"480\">\n</iframe>","descriptionType":"text/html","publishedDate":"Fri, 21 Aug 2020 10:00:00 +0000","feedId":4497,"bgimg":"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597885022491-G9CCQW6UL02DVANVQVLC/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w","linkMd5":"c3c9b72c1dfd0740aa4dcdb0cd235429","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn1@2020_2/2020/08/24/22-03-03-114_db6fa90fbf4334c3.webp","destWidth":1000,"destHeight":563,"sourceBytes":90507,"destBytes":57332,"author":"Tommy Williams","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597885022491-G9CCQW6UL02DVANVQVLC/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn1@2020_2/2020/08/24/22-03-03-114_db6fa90fbf4334c3.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598306582860},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","title":"Ray Fisher Says Warner Bros. Thank you @WarnerMedia and @ATT for making strides to ensure a safer workplace for all!”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Well, it will be interesting to see what will come of this. The movie was described as being a gritty 70s war movie, and you definitely get that vibe in this poster art that was shared.</p><p class=\"\">The two posters might look the same, but there is one difference that I noticed. This upsets a lot of people who do wear masks.</p><p class=\"\">It’s really strange to see people getting in fights and arguments over these protective masks. The series will follow “an unreliable narrator who nurses brain tumors he does not have and mourns family members who are not dead while preying on people’s sympathy to get away with almost anything.”</p><p class=\"\">Bravo will co-write the pilot with <strong>Brian Savelson</strong>. Bravo said in a statement:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“What may have started out as my dog ate homework turns into my mother died of cancers, my brother took his life and I have a double doctorate. Our protagonist is white, male and pathological. There is a void in him and he fills it by duping people. He’s a scammer. The series examines white identity and how we as an audience participate in making room for this behavior. Getting to partner with Annapurna and Nine Stories is a gift and I am most thrilled for what lies ahead.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">This certainly sounds like an interesting story and it will be a great project for Gyllenhaal to jump into and be a part of. Finally, the Theater District is where you’ll be able to watch the finalists for Hime’s Cosplay Cup on September 5.</p><p class=\"\">Fans will also want to check out the Super Arcade where you’ll be able to find additional awesome content like anime <strong>Idris Elba</strong> and <strong>John Boyega</strong>.</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">“Onyx Equinox” Scavenger Hunt: Fans can play on the Virtual Crunchyroll Expo app starting September 3 to win a year of Crunchyroll Premium or tickets to CRX 2021.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Gallery Tour featuring MAPPA: This will be an inside look at some Studio MAPPAs biggest hits, alongside behind-the-scenes commentary from Sunghoo Park (Director, “The God of High School”).</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Anime Runs Deep: A Celebrity Fan Exhibit: Crunchyroll will share some anime-inspired interpretations of celebrities who a big anime fans  like Idris Elba (Actor, “Thor” &#38; “The Wire”), John Boyega (Actor, “Star Wars” sequel trilogy films), and LJ Collier (Athlete, Seattle Seahawks)</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Yuzu's Cat Cafe: A 24/7 live stream of kittens from The Kitten Academy where fans can donate or adopt a cat of their own.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Anime Rave: Each night of the show fans can listen to music from DJs on Twitch and dance the night away.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Virtual Schwag: There will be cosplay backgrounds, posters, as well as virtual item giveaways from some of our industry panels.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Quiet Rooms: A place for fans to unwind with laid-back music and see anime artwork from “Tower of God”, “Somali and the Forest Spirit,” and “Laid-Back Camp.”</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Hatsune Miku Symphony Orchestra Concert: The Miku Symphony is celebrating its 5th anniversary with this special performance by vocaloid Miku Hatsune and the Tokyo Philharmonic Orchestra.</p></li></ul><p class=\"\">V-CRX will begin at 10 AM PT on September 4 and run until 10 PM PT on September 6. She’d had a brain tumor removed, and her children blamed it for her actions; the media took a darker view of her during a sensationalized affair, depicting her as a hot-blooded woman scorned and dubbing her ‘Black Widow.’ She served 18 years in jail before being let out in 2016.”</p><p class=\"\">The film is currently casting the rest of the roles, and <a href=\"https://deadline.com/2020/08/mgm-ridley-scott-lady-gaga-gucci-film-robert-de-niro-jared-leto-al-pacino-adam-driver-reeve-carney-1202997254/\">Deadline</a> reports that Scott and the casting directors are in talks with <strong>Robert De Niro</strong>, <strong>Al Pacino</strong>, <strong>Adam Driver</strong>, and <strong>Jared Leto</strong>, as well as <strong>Jack Huston</strong> (<em>Boardwalk Empire</em>, <em>Fargo</em>) and <strong>Reeve Carney</strong> (<em>Penny Dreadful</em>). />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">A couple of years ago, a report surfaced that DC Entertainment was developing a two-part animated film adaptation of <strong>Jeph Loeb</strong> and <strong>Tim Sale</strong>'s&#160;<strong><em>Batman: The Long Halloween</em></strong>. Well, that was officially confirmed by  actor <strong>Matt Bomer </strong>during&#160;<a href=\"https://www.ign.com/articles/batman-the-long-halloween-animated-movie-confirmed\" target=\"_self\">IGN</a>’s <em>Superman: Man of Tomorrow&#160;</em>panel that took place during DC FanDome.</p><p class=\"\">This is one of my favorite Batman stories! It’s a story that I would have loved to see adapted as a live-action feature, but of course, I’ll take a two-part animated film! Hopefully, they stick to the story that the comic tells. The DC animated films are decent, but I want this one to be a top-notch adaptation in every way.</p><p class=\"\">If you’re not familiar with the story for some reason, here’s a synopsis:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\"><em>Christmas. St. Patrick’s Day. Easter. As the calendar’s days stack up, so do the bodies littered in the streets of Gotham City. A murderer is loose, killing only on holidays. The only man that can stop this fiend? The Dark Knight. In a mystery taking place during Batman’s early days of crime fighting,&#160;Batman: The Long Halloween&#160;is one of the greatest Dark Knight stories ever told.&#160;</em></p><p class=\"\"><em>Working with District Attorney Harvey Dent and Lieutenant James Gordon, Batman races against the calendar as he tries to discover who Holiday is before he claims his next victim each month. A mystery that has the reader continually guessing the identity of the killer, this story also ties into the events that transform Harvey Dent into Batman’s deadly enemy, Two-Face.</em>“</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">It was previously reported that this will be a standalone project and will not connect to any of the previous DC animated films. Written by <strong>Kyle Newman</strong>, <strong>Mike Witwer</strong>, and <strong>Jon Peterson</strong>, <strong><em>Heroes’ Feast: The Official Dungeons &#38; Dragons Cookbook</em></strong> includes a wide array of recipes like biscuits, stew, ribs, and so much more.</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">80 recipes inspired by the magical world of Dungeons &#38; Dragons–perfect for a solo quest or a feast shared with fellow adventurers.</p><p class=\"\">From the D&#38;D experts behind Dungeons &#38; Dragons Art &#38; Arcana comes a cookbook that invites fantasy lovers to learn about their favorite fictional cultures through their unique cuisines and lifestyles. With this book, you can prepare dishes delicate enough to dine like elves and their drow cousins or hearty enough to feast like a dwarven clan or a boisterous orcish horde. All eighty dishes–developed by a professional chef from one of the country’s top test kitchens–are delicious, easy to prepare, and composed of wholesome ingredients readily found in our world.</p><p class=\"\">Heroes’ Feast includes recipes for snacking, such as Bytopian Shepherd’s Bread, Iron Rations, savory Hand Pies, and Hogs in Bedrolls, as well as hearty vegetarian, meaty, and fish mains, such as Amphail Braised Beef, Hommlet Golden Brown Roasted Turkey, Drow Mushroom Steaks, and Moonshae Seafood Risotto. There are also featured desserts and cocktails–like Heartlands Roseapple &#38; Blackberry Pie, Yawning Portal Biscuit, and Chultan Zombie–and everything in between, to satisfy a craving for any adventure.</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Fans will be able to grab <em>Heroes’ Feast</em> on October 27 from your favorite retailers. You can even <a href=\"https://www.penguinrandomhouse.com/books/645417/heroes-feast-by-kyle-newman-jon-peterson-and-michael-witwer/\" target=\"_blank\">pre-order</a> your copy now. the crews have been hard at work getting the new attraction, Avengers Campus, ready at Disney’s California Adventure park. The attraction was supposed to be opening this summer, but just like everything else, it got put on hold when the pandemic struck. But they are making headway, and we have a few new pictures of the progress!</p><p class=\"\">The Instagram account <a href=\"https://www.instagram.com/waltdisneyimagineering/?utm_source=ig_embed\">Walt Disney Imagineering</a> put out some new photos of the Stark Quinjet arriving at the park, as well as the new attraction insignia for<em> Web Slingers: A Spider-Man Adventure</em>. This is pretty exciting! </p><p class=\"\">Here’s the description for the attraction:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">The Avengers<em> are setting up new Headquarters and training facilities around the globe to inspire all potential recruits willing to step up and become something more. As part of this global initiative, Tony Stark has founded the Worldwide Engineering Brigade — or WEB for short— to develop advancements in super-powered technology, including new enhancements to Spider-Man’s suit as their debut project. By bringing together the world’s brightest young inventors, the WEB is creating new interfaces that will empower all of us to join the ranks of Earth’s Mightiest.</em></p></blockquote><p class=\"\">My family was lucky enough to visit the Disney parks in December, and it was cool to see the area coming together that will house all this awesomeness. class=\"\">&#160;Netflix has released the trailer for a fun little romantic comedy titled <strong><em>Love, Guaranteed</em></strong>. But Susan and Nick soon find themselves in the middle of a media storm, and as the case heats up, so do their feelings for each other—which could jeopardize everything.&#160;</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The cast for the film also includes <strong>Heather Graham</strong>,&#160;<strong>Quynh Mi</strong>,&#160;<strong>Jed Rees</strong>,&#160;<strong>Lisa Durupt</strong>, and&#160;<strong>Brendan Taylor</strong>. The studio is currently in talks with director&#160;<strong>J.C. Chandor </strong>to helm the film. Chandor is the director of films such as <em>Triple Frontier, A Most Violent Year, All Is Lost</em>, and <em>Margin Call</em>.</p><p class=\"\">Chandor has made some solid films in his career — they’re actually all well-made films, but <em>Kraven The Hunter </em>will be his first big tentpole movie. I think he could deliver something pretty cool, something that the fans will appreciate. But we’ll have to wait and see.</p><p class=\"\">It would make sense to see Kraven get his own movie. Not only is it a character that fans have been wanting to see in a film, but there have also been reports that the character could make his big-screen debut in the upcoming third solo<em> Spider-Man</em> movie. After all, he is one of Spider-Man’s best known and most formidable enemies. </p><p class=\"\">The Spider-Man sequel could take story points from <em>Kraven's Last Hunt</em>&#160;comic, which was written by&#160;<strong>J. M. DeMatteis</strong>, first published in 1997. It’s one of the best Spider-Man stories that has been created. It tells&#160;the story of Spider-Man's final battle with Kraven The Hunter. Here’s the description of that comic.</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">Kraven the Hunter has stalked and killed every animal known to man. But there is one beast that has eluded him. One quarry that has mocked him at every turn: the wall-crawling web-slinger known as Spider-Man. And to prove that he is the hero's master, he will pull on his costume and become him... after he shoots and buries him six feet under!&#160;</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">In a <a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/kraven-the-hunter-will-reportedly-appear-in-the-next-spider-man-movie\" target=\"_blank\">previously released</a> casting description, the character is described as being of Russian origin, with \"superhuman strength, speed, stamina, agility, and reflexes.\" It goes on to say that this&#160;\"maniacal big-game hunter seeks to defeat Spider-Man to prove that he is the greatest hunter in the world.\" The studio is looking for an actor in the 35-50 age range to play the character, who is also described as a \"Bourne-like bounty hunter.”</p><p class=\"\">The script for the film was written by <strong>Richard Wenk</strong>, who penned&#160;<em>The Equalizer</em>&#160;films for Sony. <strong>Matt Tolmach </strong>and <strong>Avi Arad </strong>are set to produce. I’m excited to see that this movie is actually moving forward. Hopefully, Sony and Chandor do something great with it. I’m curious to see what kind of standalone story they end up telling with Kraven. />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">Disney is getting ready for the debut of <strong><em>Phineas and Ferb The Movie: Candace Against the Universe</em></strong> on Disney+ next week. One thing they’re doing to celebrate is by creating adorable little shorts that are in the style of chibis. This takes fun characters and makes them ridiculously adorable. There will be three of these specials which will air on Disney Channel during a multi-day <strong><em>Phineas and Ferb</em></strong> marathon that will run on August 22 and 23 from 10 AM-4 PM ET/PT.</p><p class=\"\">The shorts collection called <strong><em>Chibi Tiny Tales: Phineas and Ferb</em></strong>. In the first one, “Rollercoaster,” fans will be treated to a retelling of the first episode. However, one thing to note is that Doofenshmirtz’s plot is vastly different. Here are the other two shorts that we’ll enjoy:</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">\"Freeze-inator Fiasco\" - When Dr. Doofenshmirtz decides to zap the sun with his 'Freeze-inator,' Perry the Platypus must come to the rescue.</p></li><li><p class=\"\">\"Run, Candace, Run\" - After Candace spots her brothers digging up dinosaur bones, she chases her mom throughout town trying to bust them.</p></li></ul>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  \n\n    \n  \n    \n\n      \n\n      \n        <figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597960096831-3YZN9AL7TJBLHHY5FRK2/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kJRqFJ19D4P4EwsC9z3fiewUqsxRUqqbr1mOJYKfIPR7LoDQ9mXPOjoJoqy81S2I8N_N4V1vUb5AoIIIbLZhVYy7Mythp_T-mtop-vrsUOmeInPi9iDjx9w8K4ZfjXt2dkV64dCjSK7Zaaf7dwPYPO_gHf_vjqrS5WJoq1nmwotrP7cJNZlDXbgJNE9ef52e8w/image-asset.jpeg\" data-image-dimensions=\"1600x900\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f3eef9fe1c2871d84ac44d4\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597960096831-3YZN9AL7TJBLHHY5FRK2/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kJRqFJ19D4P4EwsC9z3fiewUqsxRUqqbr1mOJYKfIPR7LoDQ9mXPOjoJoqy81S2I8N_N4V1vUb5AoIIIbLZhVYy7Mythp_T-mtop-vrsUOmeInPi9iDjx9w8K4ZfjXt2dkV64dCjSK7Zaaf7dwPYPO_gHf_vjqrS5WJoq1nmwotrP7cJNZlDXbgJNE9ef52e8w/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">I’ve only seen “Rollercoaster,” but I absolutely love it. The art is so adorable and fun. I think my favorite is Doofenshmirtz. He’s just so cute, there’s no way he’s truly evil.</p><p class=\"\">In addition, Disney XD will be airing every <em>Phineas and Ferb</em> episode, short, and movie starting on August 25 at 6 AM ET/PT. 06:03:02","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","title":"Review: Fight, Die And Fight Again In MORTAL SHELL","link":"https://geektyrant.com/news/review-fight-die-and-fight-again-in-mortal-shell","description":"<figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597688918909-JCIWPMQHUWQIYNUVELQE/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kBvUr1GNyopL67xe7lGlyIkUqsxRUqqbr1mOJYKfIPR7LoDQ9mXPOjoJoqy81S2I8N_N4V1vUb5AoIIIbLZhVYxCRW4BPu10St3TBAUQYVKcyMX9KsLNqYZ7J5RfalIAFv6PX8nPAgFJ6hPr9oYEr9z3h9ERiYLbnpA3h8yuxtNA/mortal-shell-hands-on-preview-a-gooey-hack-n-slash-center_feature.jpg\" data-image-dimensions=\"1166x656\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"mortal-shell-hands-on-preview-a-gooey-hack-n-slash-center_feature.jpg\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f3acc564ae84a1f6b55400b\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597688918909-JCIWPMQHUWQIYNUVELQE/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kBvUr1GNyopL67xe7lGlyIkUqsxRUqqbr1mOJYKfIPR7LoDQ9mXPOjoJoqy81S2I8N_N4V1vUb5AoIIIbLZhVYxCRW4BPu10St3TBAUQYVKcyMX9KsLNqYZ7J5RfalIAFv6PX8nPAgFJ6hPr9oYEr9z3h9ERiYLbnpA3h8yuxtNA/mortal-shell-hands-on-preview-a-gooey-hack-n-slash-center_feature.jpg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">With many games following similar footsteps and the paved path that the Souls series has made, it’s hard to find those that are worth your time and energy playing. Mortal Shell is both an homage to the Souls series and a well crafted set of original ideas. There are some issues with a lack of variety, funky AI and some confusing environments, but the overall experience is tough, fun and inviting.</p><p class=\"\">For all intents and purposes, this is a Souls game. Players wander an unknown land with nothing but some weapons, armor and items found scattered around the world. The major difference in this game is the new and unique defense mechanism where the character will harden their bodies and be able to endure practically any physical damage once. It’s continually interesting because it can be used in the middle of dodge roles, attacks, running and anything else possible. This allows players to be a little more daring in their fights and rewarding well timed and thought out attacks.I used a simple pattern, attack, harden, the enemy would flinch, attack again then back away to have everything cool down and I’d do it again. I basically used this pattern through most if not all of my play through. It was deeply satisfying and fun to be able to initiate and have battles like this, but it did become stale after hours of doing it and not finding much of a better way to combat enemies. This is a Souls like game, so it makes sense to be careful and such, but other mechanics or other ways to use my “harden” ability would have been a good touch to add variety and personalization in gameplay.</p><p class=\"\">Another major difference is that as players are battling, if they take a fatal attack then their bodies are knocked out of the “shell” that they are inhabiting and have a chance to finish off an enemy and return to the shell and re-inhabit it. This can be hugely advantageous in a difficult battle or help newer players because they can lose all their health and regain it all as they inhabit the body again. This added layer of strategy for advanced players and forgiveness for novices is another great touch in the game.</p><p class=\"\">Talking about the different shells players can inhabit, each “shell” has its own abilities, unique stats and other things. Between weapons and the shells, it’s great to have some core variety in the game. I wish that players were able to get to these new weapons and shells a little sooner. I also would have loved to see maybe one or two more shells and some more weapons, the game is fine with the selection now, but it could have used more to make combat more diverse.</p><p class=\"\">Mortal Shell has lots of mystery and pushes players to experiment. This includes experimenting with unknown items, exploration and other things. However, the game could guide a little bit better or be a little bit easier on players who are trying new items or exploring obscure places. Mystery in lore and rewarding experimentation during combat and using items is great, but punishing players for just trying out items seems a little unfair.&#160;</p><p class=\"\">Overall this game is definitely a challenge for newcomers, but is still more welcoming and approachable than some of the more intense Souls games. It demands and asks a lot of his players and that can be quite daunting for most people. However, if you are a fan of Souls like games or want to try and get into them, Mortal Shell is an overall good experience.</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  \n\n    \n  \n    \n\n      \n\n      \n Girls</em></strong> is getting a live-action series adaptation thanks to The CW. This is an animated series that I enjoyed watching with my girls when they were younger. It was a fun series and it’s pretty crazy that it’s getting the live-action treatment. </p><p class=\"\">The series will center on the titular superheroes who “are now&#160;disillusioned twentysomethings who resent having lost their childhood to crime fighting. Will they agree to reunite now that the world needs them more than ever?”</p><p class=\"\">That could actually be fun. The original animated series was created by<strong> Craig McCracken</strong>. In the story, Professor Utonium accidentally created the elementary school aged super team of Blossom, Bubbles, and Buttercup by combining sugar, spice, and everything nice with the mysterious Chemical X. </p><p class=\"\">The show ran for six seasons between 1998 and 2005. There was also a <em>Powerpuff Girls</em> movie that was released in 2002, and a rebooted animated series that came to Cartoon Network in 2016.</p><p class=\"\">The live-action series is being developed by producers <strong>Diablo Cody</strong> (Juno) and <strong>Greg Berlanti</strong> (All the DC TV shows). The game was created by 3 Australian comedians (<strong>Ray Cashman</strong>, <strong>Peter Gleeson</strong>, and <strong>Seizure Kaiser</strong>) and is all about having fun as you and up to 3 of your friends face off against each other.</p><p class=\"\"><em>Power Slam!</em> is currently on <a href=\"https://www.kickstarter.com/projects/powerslamcardgame/power-slam-wrestling-card-game\" target=\"_blank\">Kickstarter</a> with roughly a week left and it has been fully funded, so no need to worry on that front. The game features fun artwork and multiple game modes to help improve the replayability. The team is hoping that <em>Power Slam!</em> will be able to ship out in time for the holidays. />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">It’s that time of the month where streaming services share which items are coming to their service and which are leaving. Netflix has shown off their list and it includes some interesting adds. I’m a little surprised to see <strong><em>The Muppets</em></strong> and <strong><em>Muppets Most Wanted</em></strong> on this list instead of on Disney+. I was also taken way back when I saw <strong><em>Sister, Sister</em></strong> is coming to the streaming service. Anyone else remember watching that back in the 90s? One of the big additions for the month of September though is going to be the <strong><em>Back to the Future</em></strong> trilogy. I’m also excited for <strong><em>The Promised Neverland</em></strong>, the fourth season of <strong><em>The Good Place</em></strong>, and the addition of <strong><em>Real Steel</em></strong>. What are you most pumped for?</p><h3>Coming Soon</h3><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">ARASHI's Diary -Voyage- ep 12 -- NETFLIX DOCUMENTARY</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">In the lead-up to their 20th anniversary, the guys open up about going digital and the challenges of launching their official social media accounts.</p></li></ul></li><li><p class=\"\">GIMS: On the Record -- NETFLIX DOCUMENTARY</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Go backstage with beloved rap superstar Gims in the year leading up to his major 2019 Stade de France performance in this up-close documentary.</p></li></ul></li></ul><h3>Available September 1</h3><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Bookmarks: Celebrating Black Voices -- NETFLIX FAMILY</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Bookmarks: Celebrating Black Voices is a live-action collection of twelve five minute episodes featuring prominent Black celebrities and artists reading children's books from Black authors that highlight the Black experience. Hosted by Marley Dias (author and founder of #1000BlackGirlBooks campaign), the collection of books and conversations center around themes of identity, respect, justice, and action -- providing families a toolset to start meaningful conversations with kids about difficult topics through short-form book-based content.</p></li></ul></li><li><p class=\"\">The Boss Baby: Get That Baby! -- NETFLIX FAMILY</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">In this interactive special, you'll find your calling at Baby Corp by making choices and carrying out missions as part of a virtual aptitude test.</p></li></ul></li><li><p class=\"\">Felipe Esparza: Bad Decisions -- NETFLIX COMEDY SPECIAL</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Stand-up comedian, actor and “Last Comic Standing” winner Felipe Esparza digs deeper into his past in his first Netflix Original comedy specials, Felipe Esparza: Bad Decisions and Felipe Esparza: Malas Decisiones. Filmed in Santa Ana, California as two separate performances – one in English and one in Spanish – the specials showcase Esparza’s edgy style of humor as the perfect vehicle to weave through difficult anecdotes of his childhood and mistakes in his adult life with ease. In each themed episode, six contestants belt out the biggest hits from that genre while being judged by a vocal analyzer comparing their vocal performance to the original artist’s. The more they sing in tune, the more cash they add to a collective jackpot worth up to $60,000. The first round is worth $10,000 and lyrics are randomly assigned so contestants must be ready for anything - the highest scoring contestant moves on, while the remaining singers vote one fellow contestant out. For five more rounds, the stakes get higher and the jackpot gets bigger, and the final two contestants face off in a head-to-head battle to win the grand prize. Perfect for an at-home sing-a-long, viewers of all ages will find themselves off the couch, belting their favorite tunes and having a sing-off of their own.</p></li></ul></li></ul><h3>Available September 17</h3><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Dragon’s Dogma -- NETFLIX ANIME</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Resurrected as an Arisen, Ethan sets out to vanquish the Dragon that took his heart, but with every demon he battles, the more he loses his humanity.</p></li></ul></li><li><p class=\"\">The Last Word -- NETFLIX ORIGINAL</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">In the aftermath of her husband’s death, a woman unexpectedly finds a new source of energy and a lust for life – as she becomes a professional eulogist to the surprise of her family and friends.</p></li></ul></li></ul><h3>Available September 18</h3><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">American Barbecue Showdown -- NETFLIX ORIGINAL</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">American Barbecue Showdown is an eight episode food competition series that follows the country’s best backyard smokers and competitive barbecuers as they compete for the title of American Barbecue Champion. Through emotional and in-depth interviews, each coach reveals the critical moments in their personal lives and careers that ultimately helped form their coaching philosophies. Featured coaches include the Los Angeles Clippers' Doc Rivers; two-time FIFA World Cup-winning coach Jill Ellis, the winningest coach in U.S. soccer history; Premier League’s José Mourinho, one of the most decorated football managers of all time; Serena Williams’ famed tennis coach, Patrick Mouratoglou; and hall of fame basketball player and coach Dawn Staley. The Playbook is produced by SpringHill Company, Delirio Films and Boardwalk Pictures.</p></li></ul></li><li><p class=\"\">Mighty Express -- NETFLIX FAMILY</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">In a playful world crisscrossed by railway tracks, a team of locomotives and their kid pals keep things moving and get deliveries through no matter what!</p></li></ul></li></ul><h3>Available September 23</h3><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Enola Holmes -- NETFLIX FILM</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">When Enola Holmes — Sherlock’s teen sister — discovers her mother missing, she sets off to find her, becoming a super-sleuth in her own right as she outwits her famous brother and unravels a dangerous conspiracy around a mysterious young Lord.</p></li></ul></li><li><p class=\"\">Waiting…</p></li></ul><h3>Available September 24</h3><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">The Chef Show: Season 2 -- NETFLIX DOCUMENTARY</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">The Chef Show returns for another season as Jon Favreau (Director/actor) and award-winning Chef Roy Choi come back together to continue learning, sharing, and celebrating different flavors, cultures and people. This new set of accessories includes a rubber game mat, a portfolio, card sleeves, and a card case all featuring the alternate art for Dark Magician Girl the Dragon Knight. I personally think that these all look great, especially the mat. </p><p class=\"\">The portfolio will come with 10 pages that hold nine cards on either side for a total of 180 cards being stored. The sleeves will come in packs of 50 which is annoying to me as that’s not enough for your side or extra decks, but also just gives you 10 more sleeves than most people use for their main deck. Could they really not have done a minimum of 60? At least then you get enough for 4 extra decks. </p><p class=\"\">Finally, the card case can fit 70 sleeved cards, so there’s plenty of room for your main, side, and extra decks with a divider there for separating cards as needed.</p><p class=\"\">All of these accessories will be available on February 5, 2021. The extremely reasonable prices are as follows:</p><ul data-rte-list=\"default\"><li><p class=\"\">Game Mat - $14.99</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Duelist Portfolio - $9.99</p></li><li><p class=\"\">Card data-image-dimensions=\"1920x1080\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f43d5300d534b51d9afe5c4\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1598281010510-CQ8EH3XFWD191POM7KZB/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\"><strong>The Suicide Squad</strong> director <strong>James Gunn</strong> has shared 17 new posters for the upcoming DC film! The posters spotlight that crazy awesome epic cast of characters that is going to fill this story. We were warned not to get too attached to any of them. The main poster with all of the characters came with the following note from Gunn on <a href=\"https://twitter.com/JamesGunn/status/1297588419959259136?ref_src=twsrc%5Etfw%7Ctwcamp%5Etweetembed%7Ctwterm%5E1297588419959259136%7Ctwgr%5E&#38;ref_url=https%3A%2F%2Fwww.comingsoon.net%2Fmovies%2Fnews%2F1146498-new-the-suicide-squad-poster\" target=\"_blank\">Twitter</a>:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">#DCFanDome is over, but #TheSuicideSquad lives on... at least until a good amount of them get massacred in August 2021. I can't tell you guys how moved &#38; grateful I am by all your support &#38; compliments yesterday. Thank you!</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The roster of characters includes <strong>Idris Elba</strong> as Bloodsport, <strong>Viola Davis </strong>as Amanda Waller, <strong>Margot Robbie </strong>as Harley Quinn,<strong> Jai Courtney </strong>as Captain Boomerang, <strong>Joel Kinnaman</strong> as Rick Flagg, <strong>David Dastmalchian</strong> as Polka-Dot Man, <strong>Steve Agee </strong>as King Shark, and<strong> Daniela Melchior </strong>as Ratcatcher, <strong>Michael Rooker</strong> as Savant, <strong>Flula Borg </strong>as Javelin, <strong>Nathan Fillion</strong> is T.D.K., <strong>Mayling Ng </strong>as Mongal,<strong> Peter Capaldi </strong>as The Thinker, <strong>Alice Braga</strong> as Sol Soria, <strong>Steve Agee </strong>as King Shark, <strong>John Cena </strong>as Peacemaker, <strong>Joaquín Cosío </strong>as Mayor General Mateo Suarez, <strong>Pete Davidson</strong> as Blackguard,<strong> Sean Gunn </strong>as Weasel, <strong>Jennifer Holland</strong> as Emilia Harcourt, <strong>Storm Reid </strong>as Bloodsport's daughter, Tyla, and more. <strong>Taika Waititi </strong>will also be in the film, but his character is not included in this video.</p><p class=\"\">While we still don’t know the main plot of the film, it was explained that<em> The Suicide Squad</em> will be like a gritty 1970’s style war action movie and Gunn also said that \"<em>The Suicide Squad</em>&#160;is by far the most fun I've ever had making a movie\" and he was looking to bring to life \"great DC villains,\" in the film whether they were are part of Task Force X in the comics or not.</p><p class=\"\">As we’ve seen in the<a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/awesome-behind-the-scenes-promo-video-for-james-gunns-the-suicide-squad\" target=\"_blank\"> behind-the-scenes video</a>, this movie looks like it’s going to be an incredibly fun flick! <em>The Suicide Squad</em> lands in theaters in 2021. However, every good adventure needs a good hook. Making an interesting or engaging plot hook can be really hard. Well, <strong>Robert Arden</strong> has created <strong><em>100 Plot Hooks</em></strong> to help DMs out. Inside this unofficial supplement, DMs will find 100 plot hooks organized by what type of quest you want the hook to feed into. </p><p class=\"\">Do you want an escort mission? An escape mission? Maybe you want an assassination mission. This is a great tool even if you don’t use any of the hooks provided to serve as inspiration for your own hook. Definitely a something DMs should consider adding to their toolbox.</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">100 Plot Hooks is a reference guide for Dungeon Masters that need a quick idea to spark some inspiration. The show delivers some funny comedy, and it’s fairly cheap to make, so I don’t think Tosh will have a problem finding a new home for it.</p><p class=\"\">Tosh joked about the cancelation, saying, “I look forward to doing an animated reboot of my show on MTV in 25 years.” As you know, the network is currently rebooting <em>Beavis and Butt-Head&#160;</em>and<em>&#160;The Ren &#38; Stimpy Show</em>. </p><p class=\"\">The 12th season of <em>Tosh.0</em> premieres on September 15 and it will reach 300 episodes, having run for 11 years.
