We’re designing all these worlds, building these villages, we’re making thousands of costumes and props, training the horses the things they’ll need to do, designing the shots of the films. There’s a lot more storyboarding. Generally I only storyboard the scenes that have visual effects or animals and stunts, things where all the departments need to be on the same page for it to work out. But this movie there is rarely a scene that isn’t on a boat or doesn’t have a lot of extras. We’re storyboarding most of the film, which is taking a lot of time and we’re continuing to do that now on this hiatus.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Eggers is one hell of a talented director. />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\"><strong>Yeon Sang-ho</strong>, the director of the Korean zombie thriller<strong><em> Train of Busan </em></strong>and its follow-up film <strong><em>Peninsula</em></strong>, is developing another sequel and that sequel will be an animated film!</p><p class=\"\">The first film, <em>Train of Busan</em>, was a great movie! I haven’t seen the sequel yet, which was recently released, but those who have seen it seem to love it! Before these two films were made, Sang-ho made an animated prequel titled <strong><em>Seoul Station</em></strong>, which told the story of how the zombie plague that devastates South Korea began.</p><p class=\"\">Sang-ho was actually working in animation before he jumped in to make these live-action movies, and for the next one, he’s decided to go back to his roots, and he’s already working on it. In a recent interview with <a href=\"https://www.polygon.com/2020/8/20/21376209/train-to-busan-peninsula-interview-animated-prequel-movie\" target=\"_blank\">Polygon</a>, the filmmaker revealed that the movie will be a prequel to<em> Peninsula</em>:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“A prequel to&#160;Peninsula: we are currently in talks about making a cartoon about the relationship between Unit 631 and Min-jung. I am hopeful that the story can be further expanded upon through the less inhibited cartoon medium.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">I love the fact that the universe is going to continue to be expended in animated form. In this case, it will dive into the stories of the character Min-jung, the mother of two young girls who rescue Jung-seok.</p><p class=\"\">When talking about coming up with his concept for<em> Peninsula</em>, the filmmaker said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“I wanted to make a post-apocalyptic movie with a devastated Korea. I also imagined a story of a young child driving a dump truck in the ruined Korea.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">When discussing the story for <em>Peninsula </em>he said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“The story is about how one is able to find hope in a peninsula that has become isolated and full of despair. The main character, Jung-seok, escaped from the peninsula once before and then lived in a world without hope, so he returns to the peninsula again. I made the movie with the intent to show that Jung-seok was not trying to escape from a geopolitical world, but from a community that was full of selfishness.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">I’m looking forward to watching the sequel, and now I can look forward to the new animated prequel being developed. For those of you who haven’t seen the original animated movie, <em>Seoul Station</em>, you can check it out below.</p><iframe scrolling=\"no\" data-image-dimensions=\"854x480\" allowfullscreen=\"\" </strong>will once again reprise his role as Bruce Wayne/Batman in Warner Bros.’ upcoming DC movie <strong><em>The Flash</em></strong>! I’m seriously shocked by the news, but happy about it! I actually liked Affleck’s version of Batman! So, the fact that we’ll get to see him expand on that role is pretty cool.</p><p class=\"\">According to <a href=\"https://deadline.com/2020/08/ben-affleck-to-return-as-batman-in-upcoming-flash-movie-1203018972/\" target=\"_blank\">Deadline</a>, it will be a cameo role and it will be alongside Michael Keaton, who is also reprising his role as Batman from the <strong>Tim Burton</strong>-directed films.</p><p class=\"\">While it is said to be just a cameo, <em>The</em>&#160;<em>Flash&#160;</em>director <strong>Andy Muscietti</strong> describes it a a “substantial” part.&#160;Affleck reportedly got the script for&#160;<em>The Flash&#160;</em>last week and agreed to jump on board the project. Muschietti said in a statement:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“He’s a very substantial part of the emotional impact of the movie. The interaction and relationship between Barry and Affleck’s Wayne will bring an emotional level that we haven’t seen before. It’s Barry’s movie, it’s Barry’s story, but their characters are more related than we think. They both lost their mothers to murder, and that’s one of the emotional vessels of the movie. That’s where the Affleck Batman kicks in.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Another reason why Affleck’s Batman needs to come back in<em>The Flash </em>is because Miller’s Flash considers him to be the original Dark Knight, the guy he fought alongside in&#160;<em>Justice League.&#160;</em>According to Muschietti, it was necessary to have Affleck’s Batman as a starting point: </p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“He’s the baseline. He’s part of that unaltered state before we jump into Barry’s adventure…There’s a familiarity there.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Well, shit. This is unexpected! But, I like it. <em>The Flash&#160;</em>is scheduled for release on June 3, 2022. <strong>Ezra Miller</strong> will be back to reprise his role. Meeting a cast of memorable characters along the way, Enola’s caught in the middle of a conspiracy that could alter the course of political history.&#160;Enola Holmes&#160;puts a dynamic new female twist on the world’s greatest detective and his brilliant family.”</p><p class=\"\">When talking about the film, director <strong>Harry Bradbeer </strong>said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“The newer spin [in this version] is that Enola Holmes hasn’t really been looked at very closely as a character. What sucks, is that this news comes after the <strong>Derek Waters</strong> and <strong>Jeremy Konner</strong> series was renewed for a seventh season last summer.</p><p class=\"\">The seventh season of&#160;<em>Drunk History</em>&#160;was in pre-production and taping some of the comedian narrations when the coronavirus pandemic shut it down. That is probably one of the reasons why the series was canceled. That and the high costs of producing the period reenactments of the show.</p><p class=\"\">On top of that, the network has been scaling down its live-action projects in favor of adult animated series. In the past couple of months, the network has announced they are developing reboots of <em>Beavis and Butt-Head and The Ren &#38; Stimpy Show&#160;</em>as well as the&#160;<em>Daria</em>&#160;spinoff<em>&#160;Jodie.</em></p><p class=\"\"><em>Drunk History&#160;</em>started out as a web series on YouTube before moving over to Funny or Die. The concept for the series entailed “an inebriated narrator, often a burgeoning comedian or UCB sketch artist, who regales an obscure historical tale which is then reenacted by famous stars. As far as reenactments, the series attracted a laundry list of guests including <strong>Tiffany Haddish, Winona Ryder, Maya Rudolph, Seth Rogen, Kirsten Dunst, Will Ferrell, Tessa Thompson, Vanessa Hudgens,&#160; Colin Hanks, Quest Love</strong> and <strong>Lin-Manuel Miranda</strong>, the latter who did an episode devoted to Alexander Hamilton.”</p><p class=\"\">The sixth and final season wrapped on August 6th, 2019, and it’s up for three Emmy nominations including Outstanding Variety Sketch series, as well as Outstanding Costumes and Production Design for a Reality/Variety/Competition series.&#160;</p><p class=\"\">This show always managed to entertain and deliver some ridiculous silly comedy. />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">Daedalic Entertainment has been developing a new video game set in <strong>J.R.R. Tolkien</strong>’s Middle Earth titled <strong><em>The Lord of the Rings: Gollum</em></strong>, and today we have our first look at the footage from the game! It’s only about a minute long, but the footage is pretty cool! </p><p class=\"\">In the trailer, we see shots of the cave that Gullom lives in, and we see him crawl out of the cave to witness that chaos of Mordor. According to IGN, the game will “mix Prince of Persia-like stealth action, feature a branching narrative, and expand on the hints given by J.R.R. Tolkien about the Stoor-formerly-known-as-Sméagol to create a brand new Lord of the Rings story that aims to fit alongside the books.”</p><p class=\"\">Daedalic Entertainment CEO <strong>Cartsen Fichtelman</strong><a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/the-lord-of-the-rings-gollum-prequel-video-game-is-confirmed-for-ps5-and-xbox-series-x\" target=\"_blank\"><strong> </strong>previously talked</a> about the game, explaining that it “follows the path of Gollum and what happens before Frodo and his companions find him trailing them in the Mines of Moria… We’ll tell his story until he first shows up. Sometimes they mention some things that happen to Gollum, but nobody knows exactly what happened. That’s our task, explaining what exactly happened there.”</p><p class=\"\">When previously talking about the gaming experience, he explained:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“When you play Gollum, you’ll play Sméagol at the same time. You need to make some decisions, maybe some decisions that are more or less from Sméagol, and some that are from Gollum. You can decide for yourself what you’d like to see more. When you decide some things, it could be—this is reflected in the mechanics. The game forces you to convince yourself and find one of these two positions. When it comes to other iconic characters in the universe, in Middle-earth, we’ll see what happens around Gollum.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">It’s also explained that it’s not just “choosing to be Sméagol or Gollum, because for Gollum as an entity it’s not that easy. Each personality is being attacked by the other; each has to defend himself.” It’s also explained that “the decisions you make affect the way the game feels. You always either play as Sméagol or as Gollum as the 'dominant' persona and that can influence animations, soundscapes, certain gameplay situations, and in-game dialogue.”</p><p class=\"\">It was also made clear that the game will not change any of the source material. It just expands on it. Lead narrative designer <strong>Tilman Schanen</strong> explains:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“We naturally stay within certain limits. It won’t be like you’re going to end up destroying Middle-earth because you never made a Sméagol choice. In the end, of course, Gollum's fate is pretty much determined by the books. But your decisions can and will have effects, for example, for other NPCs in the game. Some decisions will have a bigger impact, others very little. Just as in real life.</p><p class=\"\">\"We follow Tolkien's story quite strictly and only take some freedom for purposes of gamification or sometimes simplification. Tolkien doesn't describe Gollum's story before he appears in the book in great detail. So mainly, we draw from small notes in the appendices and second-hand reports from characters like Gandalf. Since we need to fill in many gaps, it gives us quite a bit of creative freedom to pursue our narrative vision.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">When talking about way Gollum was presented in the game, he said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“With Gollum himself, our goal is to make him more relatable, as players have to be able to slip into his skin for the course of an entire game. That's why our Gollum looks less creepy (and has more hair) than the movie version.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The game is set to be released sometime in 2021, and I’ll be looking forward to watching it. 06:03:02","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","title":"Sam Raimi and His Team Secretly Recut DARKMAN Without The Studio Knowing Hours Before it Was Locked","link":"https://geektyrant.com/news/sam-raimi-and-his-team-secretly-recut-darkman-without-the-studio-knowing-48-hours","description":"<figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597984241054-2A3IFQLA8G29KA37SYRF/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg\" data-image-dimensions=\"1920x1080\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f3f4df0aa34794fc9b713d5\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597984241054-2A3IFQLA8G29KA37SYRF/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">I’m a big fan of <strong>Sam Raimi</strong>’s <strong><em>Darkman</em></strong>. For 1990 that was one hell of a good superhero film, and it might have been even better if the director actually got to edit the film the way he wanted to. Unfortunately, Universal Pictures stepped in, cut Raimi out, and hired their own editor to cut the movie together.</p><p class=\"\">Thankfully, at the last minute, Raimi and his team stepped in to re-cut the film in secret without the studio knowing until it was too late for them to make any more changes.</p><p class=\"\"><strong><em>Darkman</em></strong>&#160;starred&#160;<strong>Liam Neeson</strong>&#160;as a brilliant scientist who embarked on a mission of&#160;revenge after being&#160;burned alive and left for dead. Thanks to a failed treatment to cure his injuries he ended up with superhuman strength and abilities. This was one of the first true dark and gritty superhero films that had been made, and it wasn't based on any existing comic book.</p><p class=\"\">In a new oral history of the film’s making that was shared by&#160;<a href=\"https://www.hollywoodreporter.com/features/darkman-turns-30-liam-neeson-frances-mcdormand-and-more-remember-the-arduous-making-of-sam-raimis-influential-superhero-film?utm_source=twitter&#38;utm_medium=social\" target=\"_blank\">THR</a>, producer&#160;<strong>Rob Tapert</strong>&#160;told the story of how Universal tried and failed to boost test screening scores by bringing in their own editor:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“When Universal brought in their own editor [Bud S. Smith], they really did not want Sam in the process. Before that, we started on the preview process, scoring maybe 65 [from the audience] and we were down to maybe a 26. They felt that he had his opportunity with the original editor [David Stiven], who was so befuddled that he wanted to cut it into a romance movie. He had a breakdown and one day said, ‘I can’t do this,’ and left.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Smith ended up signing on under the condition no one was to bother him while cutting the movie, and a few weeks later he turned in a much shorter cut of the film. With every new cut the was turned in the test audience scores got lower and lower. Tapet said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“Universal sent us away. We came back, and the editor had cut it down from two hours to 85 minutes. We tested that, and it did not test as well as the longer version, which was Sam’s cut. I think we went through four or five more test screenings, and each time the score got lower and lower, and we got more depressed.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The composer&#160;of the film <strong>Danny Elfman</strong>&#160;also shared in the report that he threatened to take his name off the movie because of what Universal was doing to Raimi’s film. There were a lot of people who had Raimi’s back, but the studio wasn’t one of them.</p><p class=\"\">It was at this point that Tapert reveals that a few hours before the final cut was to be delivered, Universal settled on the shorter cut that Smith turned in. So, Tapert, Raimi, and editor&#160;<strong>Bob Murawski</strong>&#160;set out on a secret mission to recut the movie over the course of 48-hours. He said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“I don’t mind saying this now, and Sam will probably be unhappy, but the studio said, ‘There is nothing we can do to save this picture. Let’s lock it [Smith cut approved].’ So we locked the picture on Friday night at 5 p.m. We were incredibly disheartened and dispirited. And Sam’s present editor, a guy by the name of Bob Murawski, said, ‘There is a much better movie than what we are locking right now.’ So, the decision was made that we would re-edit the movie. We spent 48 hours basically recutting the entire movie, restoring things we thought were important. We added nine minutes back in, things we really liked that the preview audiences would recoil from, but that was what it was meant to do. We locked&#160;it — and didn’t tell anybody.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Universal obviously eventually found out, and they were pissed, but at this point, there was nothing they could do. The negatives were already being prepared for the press screenings:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“Universal came to watch it after the mix, and there was this giant outcry, but there was nothing to be done. The negative had been cut. Critic screenings were 48 hours later. Bob and I advocated very strongly for the deception. Sam, left to his own, probably would not have done that. He is not that kind of guy. But I am.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The movie didn’t end up being a huge hit at the time, but it did get positive reviews and it made $48 million on a $16 million budget. Unfortunately, it wasn’t Sam Raimi’s full vision, but he did get one last jab in at the studio to attempt to save his movie. Maybe we should start a campaign for #DarkmanRaimiCut!</p><p class=\"\">Knowing this story makes the movie even better for me! Raimi’s experience with <em>Darkman</em> wasn’t a good one and he even decided not to participate in this report. But, he should be proud of what he was able to give us. It really did turn out to be a solid flick, but I’d love to see what his full vision for it would have been. X-Files</em></strong> reunited with members of the creative team for a music video that was shot virtually for charity. They recorded a special version of the show’s famous theme song and it includes fan-written lyrics.</p><p class=\"\"><em>The X-Files </em>series executive producer <strong>Frank Spotnitz</strong> wanted to organize this to help the needy during the ongoing coronavirus pandemic. He challenged fans to write lyrics for the show’s instrumental theme song and the winning tune was written by fans <strong>Jennifer Large </strong>and <strong>Rebecca McDonald</strong>.</p><p class=\"\">It’s silly but fun as it brought together 33 members of “The X-Files” cast and team, including <strong>David Duchovny </strong>(Fox Mulder), <strong>Gillian Anderson</strong> (Dana Scully), <strong>Mitch Pileggi </strong>(Walter Skinner), <strong>Robert Patrick</strong> (John Doggett), <strong>Annabeth Gish</strong> (Monica Reyes), <strong>James Pickens Jr.</strong> (Alvin Kersh), <strong>Laurie Holden</strong> (Marita Covarrubias), <strong>William B. Davis </strong>(Cigarette-Smoking Man), <strong>Nicholas Lea</strong> (Alex Krycek), <strong>Cary Elwes </strong>(Brad Follmer), creator <strong>Chris Carter</strong>, executive producer-writer <strong>Vince Gilligan</strong>, composer <strong>Mark Snow</strong>, director <strong>Michelle MacLaren</strong> and many others. </p><p class=\"\">The video will raise funds for World Central Kitchen, an organization that focuses on assisting communities in crisis, to provide hot meals and creating smart solutions to hunger and poverty. The video includes a donate button and a message from Spotnitz outlining the work that the charity does.</p><p class=\"\">Chris Carter said in a statement, “We wanted to gather ‘The X-Files’ family together during these trying times to put some hope and spirit back into the world. And use the occasion to give thanks and donations to those who need it most.”</p><p class=\"\">Spotnitz add: “During lockdown I really wanted to find a way to do something positive, and we had a rare opportunity to get ‘The X-Files’ gang back together, so we hit upon this idea of putting lyrics to the theme tune – which had never been done before. It has been quite an amazing and amusing ride to put together this complex project and we’re honored that so many of our wonderful cast members and team have taken part. It’s been a real joy to reunite virtually with our friends and former colleagues, and we hope not only to bring a smile to many people, but also to help a worthwhile cause.”</p><p class=\"\">Check out KINGMAKER","link":"https://geektyrant.com/news/review-roll-through-a-journey-in-pathfinder-kingmaker","description":"<figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597533666152-NPY8BD2SJ99KP115MSQI/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/apps.64990.68573826335534875.b1ff69dd-c187-4887-8be5-65fc732add51.jpg\" data-image-dimensions=\"1920x1080\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"apps.64990.68573826335534875.b1ff69dd-c187-4887-8be5-65fc732add51.jpg\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f386de1de22531a4d87f242\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597533666152-NPY8BD2SJ99KP115MSQI/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/apps.64990.68573826335534875.b1ff69dd-c187-4887-8be5-65fc732add51.jpg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">Moving any game from one medium to another is always difficult whether it is a tabletop RPG, board game, video game, or physical sport. <strong><em>Pathfinder: Kingmaker</em></strong> is a good example of how to move a specific franchise into a new area. Between its various details and the massive amount of customization and faithfulness to the tabletop game and its very long and mostly interesting story, players can enjoy the full game and the DLCs on consoles now. There are still some issues with the core elements of the game and the move to console, but overall, fans of the <em>Pathfinder </em>franchise will be able to appreciate it and enjoy many hours of content.</p><p class=\"\">It is pretty impressive how much the character creation mirrors the physical game. They are basically identical. It can be pretty daunting for people who haven’t played<em> Pathfinder</em> or <em>Dungeons and Dragons</em>. There really should have been some more form and a structured tutorial with explanations of the character sheet and the abilities. All those initial choices heavily dictate how your character will play throughout the rest of the game. But for experienced players, everything is pretty smooth and well put together.</p><p class=\"\">The actual gameplay has a turn-based mode that can be toggled. I found it necessary to turn on the turn-based version just because it was both too fast and too slow in the other mode. Either enemies would attack without me realizing it or my characters would stand idly by too long as I was moving my cursor from ability to ability and movement. I understand that other players may be able to juggle everything really quickly and smoothly, but the nature of the<em> Pathfinder</em> game feels like it is more a turn based game than more action-oriented. I wish there was a little bit more structure and better organization for the console version. A lot of it makes sense and works well on a computer, but just like how things are changed for games like Diablo, this game could’ve used some heavy alterations to controls for console users. But once a player can figure out how to control their characters and use their abilities effectively, battles become just like any tabletop game; juggling movement, abilities, initiative, and other things.</p><p class=\"\">One of the other main issues is how long-winded some of the missions and gameplay are. When playing the tabletop version, players are actively talking to each other and the dungeon master and the flow of time in battles seem to move very quickly. But in this game, every battle felt fairly similar. And without face-to-face interactions or a dungeon master guiding and making the battles more interesting with on the spot changes, combat became somewhat bland.</p><p class=\"\">What this game comes down to is knowing what to expect from it and know what you want as a player. If you’re looking for a mostly faithful interpretation of the Pathfinder tabletop game in a digital format, then this game works really well. You lose a lot of the creativity that you’re able to have in face-to-face interactions with a group, but players can still enjoy playing through an adventure with her own character and lots of customization. If a person wants to get into table-top games, but is hesitant about the longer/socially driven games, then this might be a good test run and dive into the mechanics of a game like this. But for players who don’t know the franchise or similar games and are expecting an RPG or action-adventure, this isn’t probably going to be very enjoyable.</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  \n\n    \n  \n />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">The release of <strong><em>The New Mutants</em></strong> is fast approaching, and to tide you over, we have new promo spot to share with you along with a bit of casting trivia you might find interesting.</p><p class=\"\">It turns out that director<strong> Josh Boone</strong> initially wanted to cast <strong>Sacha Baron Cohen</strong> in the role of Warlock in the film. <a href=\"https://nerdist.com/article/new-mutants-sacha-baron-cohen-warlock-mocap/\" target=\"_blank\">Nerdist</a>&#160;reports that the filmmaker wanted Cohen to appear in the movie as essentially the \"<strong>Andy Serkis</strong> of Warlock,\" with a mo-cap performance. </p><p class=\"\">Cohen's version of Warlock ended up being scrapped due to budget constraints, so Boone was forced to choose between including Warlock or Demon Bear. Demon Bear obviously won in the end. </p><p class=\"\">When <a href=\"https://www.google.com/url?client=internal-element-cse&#38;cx=partner-pub-7101134335055522%3A5646208315&#38;q=https%3A%2F%2Fgeektyrant.com%2Fnews%2Fthere-was-a-new-mutants-sequel-in-development-with-warlock-and-karma-and-antonio-banderas-was-cast-as-the-villain&#38;sa=U&#38;usg=AOvVaw2uSfmplY9yhBKs4nOkGgxL&#38;ved=2ahUKEwi6rq-9h6jrAhXKK80KHa7jCNEQFjAAegQIAhAC\" target=\"_blank\">previously talking </a>about wanting to include Warlock in the film, Boone explained that Warlock would have eventually been introduced in the sequel. But, that sequel will probably never happen. There was a whole trilogy planned!</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">\"Karma was always going to be the villain in the second movie that would be absorbed into the group by the end. We had always wanted to bring Karma and Warlock into the second one when we couldn’t do it in the first one.\"</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Cohen as Warlock definitely would have been good casting, even if it was going to be motion capture performance work. You might like what you see, you might not. Her look reminded me of the movie <em>Cats</em>. Regardless, <em>Wonder Woman 1984 </em>looks like it could be a lot of fun! I love the first film, so I’m going to watch the sequel!</p><p class=\"\">The story for the sequel picks up with Diana Prince as she’s working at the Natural History Museum in Washington, D.C., and she’s been living a quiet, lonely life since the events of the first movie. But she’s still just trying to help the people who need it. </p><p class=\"\">The movie was directed by <strong>Patty Jenkins </strong>and it also stars <strong>Gal Godot </strong>as Diana Prince, <strong>Chris Pine</strong> as Steve Trevor,<strong> Kristen Wiig</strong> as The Cheetah, <strong>Pedro Pascal</strong> as Max Lord,<strong> Robin Wright</strong> as Antiope, and <strong>Connie Nielsen </strong>as Hippolyta. </p><p class=\"\">If you want to know more about the story the movie tells, some details were revealed in a junior novelization of the film, which you can read <a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/wonder-woman-1984-junior-novelization-reveals-how-steve-trevor-returns-and-maxwell-lords-complicated-villainous-plan\" target=\"_blank\">about here</a>. But, those details do contain spoilers. </p><p class=\"\">The movie is set to hit theaters on October 2, 2020.</p><iframe scrolling=\"no\" data-image-dimensions=\"854x480\" allowfullscreen=\"\" air and I cannot wait for the season to hit Disney+ so that I can finally watch it. </p><p class=\"\">Don’t forget to watch “The Plantars Check In” tomorrow at 8:20 PM ET/PT.</p><iframe Williams","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1597796074826-LXJ887ZTN8GBO59NZH7N/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/image-asset.jpeg?format=1000w":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn55@2020_6/2020/08/24/22-03-03-393_37c039c013954e4e.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598306582849},{"createdTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","updatedTime":"2020-08-25 06:03:02","title":"First Poster and Photos From THE HAUNTING OF BLY MANOR Which Is Season 2 of THE HAUNTING OF HILL HOUSE ","link":"https://geektyrant.com/news/first-poster-and-photos-from-the-haunting-of-bly-manor-which-is-season-2-of-the-haunting-of-hill-house","description":"<figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n              intrinsic\n            \"\n        >\n          \n        \n        \n\n        \n          \n            \n          \n            <img class=\"thumb-image\" data-image=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1598284296185-K7Q12R6AGYDTE3SJ2L5H/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/first-poster-and-photos-from-the-haunting-of-bly-manor-which-is-season-2-of-the-haunting-of-hill-house-social.jpg\" data-image-dimensions=\"1920x1080\" data-image-focal-point=\"0.5,0.5\" alt=\"first-poster-and-photos-from-the-haunting-of-bly-manor-which-is-season-2-of-the-haunting-of-hill-house-social.jpg\" data-load=\"false\" data-image-id=\"5f43e20444739f190630a362\" data-type=\"image\" src=\"https://images.squarespace-cdn.com/content/v1/51b3dc8ee4b051b96ceb10de/1598284296185-K7Q12R6AGYDTE3SJ2L5H/ke17ZwdGBToddI8pDm48kNvT88LknE-K9M4pGNO0Iqd7gQa3H78H3Y0txjaiv_0fDoOvxcdMmMKkDsyUqMSsMWxHk725yiiHCCLfrh8O1z5QPOohDIaIeljMHgDF5CVlOqpeNLcJ80NK65_fV7S1USOFn4xF8vTWDNAUBm5ducQhX-V3oVjSmr829Rco4W2Uo49ZdOtO_QXox0_W7i2zEA/first-poster-and-photos-from-the-haunting-of-bly-manor-which-is-season-2-of-the-haunting-of-hill-house-social.jpg?format=1000w\" />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">For those of you who are fans of Netflix’s incredible horror drama series <strong><em>The Haunting of&#160;Hill House</em></strong>, we’ve got our first look at the second season to share with you today! The title for the new season is&#160;<strong><em>The Haunting of Bly Manor</em></strong>, and we have a poster, some photos, and new details to share with you thanks to <a href=\"https://www.vanityfair.com/hollywood/2020/08/haunting-of-bly-manor-hill-house\" target=\"_blank\">Vanity Fair</a>.</p><p class=\"\">The photos feature several members of the cast, which includes<em> The Haunting of Hill House</em> alums <strong>Victoria Pedretti</strong>, <strong>Oliver Jackson-Cohen</strong>, <strong>Henry Thomas</strong>, and <strong>Catherine Parker</strong>.  The cast of the series also includes <strong>T’Nia Miller</strong> (<em>Years and Years</em>), <strong>Rahul Kohli </strong>(<em>iZombie</em>), <strong>Amelia Eve</strong>, <strong>Benjamin Ainsworth</strong>, and <strong>Amelie Smith </strong>(<em>EastEnders</em>).</p><p class=\"\"><strong><em>The Haunting of Bly Manor </em></strong>is said to be an adaptation of the 1898 novel by <strong>Henry James</strong>, <em>The Turn of the Screw</em>. The book tells the story of a governess, who will be played by Pedretti, who is hired to look after a pair of siblings whose parents had died. However, several ghosts around their manor house exhibit a supernatural hold over the children and the governess starts seeing the ghosts and is terrorized. </p><p class=\"\">It’s explained that while&#160;<em>Hill House</em>&#160;“was the story of family struggle and trauma,&#160;<em>Bly Manor</em>&#160;is about broken hearts that never heal and tragic star-crossed romance.” Creator and producer <strong>Mike Flanagan</strong> said:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“It certainly provides a new way to tell a love story, and there are three of them really that beat at the heart of this season. They all have a very dark edge to them. And by the end, it’s really hard to differentiate tragedy with romance. That sense of romantic longing for someone who meant so much to us—but who’s gone—really is the heart of any ghost story.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">When talking about what the foundation of these <em>Haunting</em> series are, Flanagan explained:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“At its foundation, the&#160;<em>Haunting</em>&#160;series is very much about haunted spaces and haunted people. The way we make those things dance together is really going to be what’s uniform about&#160;<em>Hill House</em>&#160;and&#160;<em>Bly. </em>Outside of that though, it was really important for all of us not to play the same notes we played for the first season. The first season is very much entrenched in family dynamics and death and grief and loss and child trauma. We all collectively felt like we’d said everything we wanted to say about that.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">When talking about the ghosts that were featured in the background in Hill House he said, “We were just trying to hide faces and figures.” But, in <em>Bly Manor</em>, he explains that the ghosts are puzzles that need to be solved:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“This season we wanted our hidden elements to tell their own story. And very much&#160;<em>unlike</em>&#160;the first season, they’re actually going to be explained. By the end of the season, you’re going to know who they are and why they’re there.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The director also <a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/mike-flanagan-discusses-haunting-of-hill-house-season-2-the-turn-of-the-screw-is-only-one-of-a-dozen-stories-were-telling\" target=\"_blank\">previously revealed</a> that the second season will adapt \"dozens\" of James’ stories as well, saying:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">\"The thing I have access to, that no other adaptation of The Turn of to the Screw has, is the rest of Henry James’ ghost stories. I get to use all of them. The Turn of the Screw has been adapted so many times. We know how perfectly it fits into a feature film format. We're doing a whole season of television. The Turn of the Screw is only one of a dozen stories that we're telling. All Henry James; all thematically linked.&#160;</p><p class=\"\">\"I think of Turning of the Screw as the backbone of this season – the through line that carries us from beginning to end. But we get to go off into The Jolly Corner and The Romance of Certain Old Clothes, and so many other of these wonderful ghost stories that people haven't seen adapted before. It's all wrapped up in what seems to be familiar, but that familiarity goes away really early in the first episode. It says, 'We're off on a whole other road.'\"</p><p class=\"\">\"It’s been really exciting to have this much bigger canvas, because you're not going to do better than The Innocents anyway.\" </p></blockquote><p class=\"\"><em>The Innocents</em> is in reference to the 1961 movie based on the same novel. This is great and the new season is also bringing back a lot of the original cast, who will all be playing different characters.</p><p class=\"\">Flanagan has <a href=\"https://geektyrant.com/news/mike-flanagan-discusses-haunting-of-hill-house-season-2-the-turn-of-the-screw-is-only-one-of-a-dozen-stories-were-telling\" target=\"_blank\">also said </a>this new season is going to be “much scarier than season one.” I’m incredibly excited for <em>Bly Manor</em>, and I hope that it ends up being just as amazing as<em> Hill House</em>!</p><p class=\"\">Check out the poster and photos from the upcoming series below.</p>\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n\n  \n\n    \n  \n    \n\n      \n\n      \n        <figure class=\"\n              sqs-block-image-figure\n Now, they’ve added five more names to the cast list for fans to enjoy. <strong>Sophie Okonedo</strong> (<em>Hotel Rwanda</em>) has been cast in the role of Amyrlin Seat Siuan Sanche. Meanwhile, <strong>Kae Alexander</strong> (<em>Game of Thrones</em>) will play Min Farshaw. In addition, the following actors will play recurring roles: <strong>Kate Fleetwood</strong> as Liandrin Guirale, <strong>Peter Franzen</strong> as Stepin, and <strong>Clare Perkins</strong> as Kerene Nagashi.</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">Based on Robert Jordan’s best-selling fantasy novels, “The Wheel of Time” is set in a high fantasy world where magic exists, but only certain women are allowed to access it. The story follows Moiraine (Rosamund Pike) as she embarks on a dangerous, world-spanning journey with five young men and women, one of whom is prophesied to be the Dragon Reborn (Josha Stradowski), a powerful individual who will either save humanity or destroy it.</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">The series showrunner is <strong>Rafe Judkins</strong>, and <strong>Uta Briesewitz</strong> is set to direct the first two episodes. Rangers</em></strong> #53 is here, and I love it! Zedd creates his Dark Rangers using a Rita clone that Finster has made. Meanwhile, Grace and Billy recharge the Dragon Coin and then have a chat where Grace refuses to let Billy tell Zordon about this. Oh boy. This is going to be something else. Also, if it goes through where they choose a Ranger instead of Zordon, I think that adds to my idea of Violet becoming the new Green Ranger instead of Drakkon. <em>MMPR</em> #53 is written by Ryan Parrott and features art by Moisés Hidalgo.</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">Lord Zedd has released his greatest creation yet-the ALL NEW DARK RANGERS; Baboo, Goldar, Squat, Finster and Rita Repulsa, powered by the Green Chaos Crystal, against the Mighty Morphin Power Rangers! What is the full extent of Lord Zedd's master plan?</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">You can grab a copy of <em>MMPR</em> #53 on August 26 from your local comic shop or through digital outlets like <a in February, although that date could very well change. However, if you need some good old Eternals fun before then, you’re in luck. Marvel recently dropped a trailer for the upcoming <strong><em>Eternals</em></strong> #1 which will start “a brand new vision of <strong>Jack Kirby</strong>’s classic Marvel creation.” <strong>Kieron Gillen</strong> is writing the series and the art comes from <strong>Esad Ribić</strong>. Gillen released the following statement:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">I said if I was ever to do a book again at Marvel, it would have to be something I've never done before. This is exactly that. This is me teaming up with literally my favourite artist of the epic, taking one of those lightning-storm Kirby visions and re-making it to be as new as the day it was forged. While Esad makes whole worlds on the page, I'm applying all the skills I've developed when I was away. It's a lot. It's everything. There's enough scale packed in here that I believe that when you look at the comic, you'll see the pages slightly bulge. Essentially 'Eternal' has to mean 'never going out of style,' which means we're aiming for 'instant classic.' Also -- fight scenes, horror, human drama, emotions, explosions. Comics!</p></blockquote><p class=\"\"><em>Eternals </em>#1 will be available from local comic stores in November. </p><blockquote class=\"twitter-tweet\"><p lang=\"en\" dir=\"ltr\">Never die. />\n          \n        \n          \n        \n\n        \n      \n        </figure>\n      \n\n    \n  \n\n\n  \n\n\n<p class=\"\">The kinds of teen sex comedies that we see these days are nothing like what they were in the 80s and 90s. A lot has changed and many of those past movies would never be made today. One of those movies is the original <strong><em>American Pie</em></strong>. </p><p class=\"\">That scene between Jim and Nadia, when Jim secretly set up his camera to stream his whole encounter with Nadia with the whole school watching them in his bedroom online, while hilarious then, would not fly today. It’s been 20 years since the movie has been made, and<strong> Shannon Elizabeth</strong>, who went topless in the film, talked about her role in the film and how she feels about doing it all these years later. Turns out, she doesn’t regret it.</p><p class=\"\">In the recently released documentary&#160;<em>Skin: A History Of Nudity In The Movies</em>, she explained:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“If I hadn’t done&#160;American Pie&#160;and I hadn’t done the role of Nadia and the nudity that came along with it, I might not have a career today.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">While she hasn’t really done much, she is obviously happy with how her career turned out. When previously talking about his scenes with Elizabeth, <strong>Jason Biggs</strong> talks about why those scenes don’t hold up after all these years, saying:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“It was a very specific time. It was right as the internet was starting. You know, we had that whole scene with the internet camera — which, by the way, would never get made now... It wouldn't get made now and it couldn't get made now. It would be unacceptable what that represents, but at the time I remember reading the script and reading that part and being shocked that there was cameras on computers! That's what I took away from it originally.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Looking back at that scene now, it’s actually pretty creepy. But, let’s be honest, all high school boys are kinda creepy. </p><blockquote data-instgrm-captioned data-instgrm-version=\"12\" class=\"instagram-media\" <strong><em>Psycho</em></strong>, he was doing something so radically different from anything that he or any other filmmaker had done before at the time. Not only was the subject matter controversial, but it was a low-budget movie that Hitchcock put his own money into because no studio wanted to fund it. </p><p class=\"\">Hitchcock staked his career and reputation on this film and luckily for him, <em>Psycho</em> ended up being a huge hit. Audiences loved it and the film is still considered a masterpiece. Psycho is a brilliant film, and the filmmaker used brilliant marketing tactics to promote it.</p><p class=\"\">One of these genius marketing moves was the trailer that he made and released for it. The six-minute trailer hardly featured any footage from the film, it mostly focused on Hitchcock giving audiences a tour of the set of the film while awesomely teasing the story. It’s one of my favorite movie trailers of all time because it breaks all conventions but also does a great job of getting audiences to want to see the movie! </p><p class=\"\">I know a lot of people who haven’t seen this trailer because they never bothered to look it up, so i thought it would be fun to share it with you. super excited about is the series adaptation of <strong>Stephen King</strong>’s <strong><em>Lisey’s Story</em></strong>. <strong>J.J. Abram</strong>s is producing the series through his Bad Robot Productions, and King is writing the scripts for all eight episodes.</p><p class=\"\">The series stars&#160;<strong>Julianne Moore</strong>, <strong>Dane DeHaan</strong>, and<strong> Clive Owen</strong>. The story follows a character named Lisey Landon and it’s set two years after her husband's death. Lisey “decides it's time to go through his office to clear out his papers. Scott Landon was a bestselling novelist and Lisey has been besieged by people wanting to buy any of his unpublished work but she is determined not to let that happen. As she begins the process of cleaning, she is contacted by an unsavory character who claims that if she does not turn over the papers, he will make her suffer the consequences. Finding strength she did not know she had and never used during their marriage, Lisey refuses, and true to his word, 'Zack McCool' begins to stalk her. Lisey begins to remember strange events from her marriage that she had suppressed and finds clues that may help save her life.\"</p><p class=\"\">The concept of the story&#160;was inspired by King’s experience when he was involved in a serious accident in June 1999. The idea for the novel sprang from a sudden realization he had when he came home from the hospital and saw that all of his belongings are in boxes. Because of that, he saw a vision of what his studio would look like after his death.</p><p class=\"\"><a href=\"https://www.comingsoon.net/tv/news/1145897-exclusive-dane-dehaan-teases-stephen-king-series-liseys-story?utm_campaign=exclusive-dane-dehaan-teases-stephen-king-series-liseys-story&#38;utm_medium=rss&#38;utm_source=rss\" target=\"_blank\">ComingSoon</a> had the opportunity to talk to DeHaan about the series. He is taking on the role of Jim Dooley a.k.a. Zack&#160;McCool in the series. With the series about to go back into production, DeHaan expresses his excitement, saying:</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“I think it’s gonna be really rad, we were doing really cool things, the set felt really good. The director’s awesome, the DP is really cool. I really hope we get to finish soon because it feels like we’re making something really wild and crazy and scary and awesome, I’m really excited about it.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">DeHaan went on to say that the details regarding his character will be different in the series than from the book. This development came from conversations between director <strong>Pablo Larrain</strong> (<em>Jackie</em>), Stephen King and the actor.</p><blockquote><p class=\"\">“He’s actually written a few scenes based on our conversations. It’s been really fun and this character, I think, will be one to remember. He’s a weird dude, and I don’t want to give too much away, but we’ve had a lot of fun taking what Stephen had in the book and bringing it to modern-day, but also in a really off-putting, strange and disgusting kind of way.”</p></blockquote><p class=\"\">Well, as long as King is the guy making the changes to the character, I’m a bit more comfortable with it. This is such a great story, and King himself said that it is one of his<em> </em>favorite books that he’s written that he would love to see adapted. Well, it’s happening and he’s the guy behind the wheel, steering the story! </p><p class=\"\">The series also stars <strong>Joan Allen</strong> (<em>A Good Marriage</em>), <strong>Sung Kang</strong> (<em>F9: The Fast Saga</em>) and <strong>Jennifer Jason Leigh </strong>(<em>The Hateful Eight</em>).
